<p><br/>
This is a list of fictional characters in the <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_(series)" title="Kirby (series)">Kirby</a></i> <a href="/wiki/Video_game" title="Video game">video game</a> series developed by <a href="/wiki/HAL_Laboratory" title="HAL Laboratory">HAL Laboratory</a> and published by <a href="/wiki/Nintendo" title="Nintendo">Nintendo</a>.</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Main_characters">Main characters</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Main characters">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Kirby">Kirby</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Kirby">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Kirby_(character)" title="Kirby (character)">Kirby (character)</a></div>
<p><b>Kirby</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">カービィ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Kābī</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a pink "puffball" who has been the star of a number of namesake games <a href="/wiki/Video_game_developer" title="Video game developer">developed</a> by <a href="/wiki/HAL_Laboratory" title="HAL Laboratory">HAL Laboratory</a>. Kirby has appeared in over twenty games since 1992 and has starred in his own animated series. The Kirby series has sold over 33 million units worldwide. The core games of the series are <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Platformer" title="Platformer">platformers</a>. The villains he encounters typically threaten his home of Dream Land <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">プププランド</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Pupupu Rando</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>, "Pupupu Land")</span> on the planet Pop Star, most often the greedy King Dedede or the mysterious Meta Knight. The main games always have Kirby with the same basic abilities; he can walk, run, jump, float, and inhale and spit out or swallow his enemies. Following <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land" title="Kirby's Dream Land">Kirby's Dream Land</a></i>, Kirby was able to gain the abilities of the enemies he swallowed, such as Fire, Sword, Fighter, and Cutter. Kirby also can spit water out of his mouth while underwater. Kirby also has had his own <a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">anime</a>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="King_Dedede">King Dedede</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: King Dedede">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/King_Dedede" title="King Dedede">King Dedede</a></div>
<p><b>King Dedede</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">デデデ大王</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Dedede Daiō</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is the primary <a href="/wiki/Villain" title="Villain">villain</a> of the series and the <a href="/wiki/Archenemy" title="Archenemy">archenemy</a> of Kirby, though he is sometimes an anti-hero. He is a large <a href="/wiki/Penguin" title="Penguin">penguin</a>-like creature who serves as the monarch of Dream Land, carrying a large wooden mallet and is known to be self-centered; furthermore, Dedede causes many problems for the inhabitants of Dream Land through selfish mischief. Despite this, he is not truly evil and does care for Dream Land. He and Kirby do not hesitate to team up against a common enemy. A recurring motif of the series is the assumption that Dedede has performed an act which is essentially benevolent, such as sealing away the villainous Nightmare from <a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Adventure" title="Kirby's Adventure">Kirby's Adventure</a>, which is misinterpreted as malevolent. Dedede often pats his belly in a jolly manner, and has many of the same abilities as Kirby himself does, such as being able to inhale objects and spit them back out with tremendous force, and the ability to suck in air and fly.</p>
<p>In the "Revenge of the King" sub-game of <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star#Remake" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star Ultra</a></i>, a harder version of King Dedede appears as <b>Masked Dedede</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">マスクド デデデ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Masukudo Dedede</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span>, wearing a distinctive combat mask and wielding a giant mechanical hammer filled with multiple weapons. This version of Dedede returns in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Triple_Deluxe" title="Kirby: Triple Deluxe">Kirby: Triple Deluxe</a></i>, having been brainwashed and strengthened by the villain Taranza.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Meta_Knight">Meta Knight</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Meta Knight">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Meta_Knight" title="Meta Knight">Meta Knight</a></div>
<p><b>Meta Knight</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">メタナイト</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Meta Naito</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is an enigmatic <a href="/wiki/Antihero" title="Antihero">antihero</a> character referred to as Kirby's rival, who often fights with him for different reasons, though they often arrive to the same goal. However, there is some discussion concerning whether or not the two are in another way related.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MetaKnightBrawl_1-0"><a href="#cite_note-MetaKnightBrawl-1">[1]</a></sup> He always wears a white-silver mask, and under it, he looks almost exactly like Kirby, though with a blue body and white eyes. He wears a navy blue cloak (The Dimensional Cape) that can transform into a set of wings, and he usually wields a special sword called the Galaxia Sword (though he gave the "Master Sword" in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_%26_the_Amazing_Mirror" title="Kirby &amp; the Amazing Mirror">Kirby &amp; the Amazing Mirror</a></i>). He follows a code of honor and usually lends Kirby a sword before they fight to be fair. Meta Knight is voiced by <a href="/wiki/Atsushi_Kisaichi" title="Atsushi Kisaichi">Atsushi Kisaichi</a> in Japan, <a href="/wiki/Eric_Stuart" title="Eric Stuart">Eric Stuart</a> in the English dub of the anime, and Eric Newsome in the English version of <i><a href="/wiki/Super_Smash_Bros._Brawl" title="Super Smash Bros. Brawl">Super Smash Bros. Brawl</a></i>. Meta Knight is often a boss and an ally of Kirby in the games. He first appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Adventure" title="Kirby's Adventure">Kirby's Adventure</a></i> in 1993, where he fights Kirby to keep him from taking a piece of the Star Rod to keep it out of Nightmare's hands.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Main_antagonists">Main antagonists</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Main antagonists">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dark_Matter">Dark Matter</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Dark Matter">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:DarkMatterKirby.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="166" data-file-width="166" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/5/56/DarkMatterKirby.jpg/150px-DarkMatterKirby.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/5/56/DarkMatterKirby.jpg 1.5x" width="150"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:DarkMatterKirby.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Dark Matter, as seen in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_2" title="Kirby's Dream Land 2">Kirby's Dream Land 2</a></i>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p><b>Dark Matter</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ダークマター</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Dāku Matā</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a species of creatures, commonly appearing as a black orb covered in orange petal-like extensions and a single red eye. It is a force of negative energy that lives a lonely existence, and it initially attacked Pop Star out of jealousy for Dream Land's lifestyle, seeking to recreate it into a dark world where no one can be happy. Dark Matter can possess other beings, putting them under its control.</p>
<p>A lone Dark Matter makes its debut in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_2" title="Kirby's Dream Land 2">Kirby's Dream Land 2</a></i> and possesses King Dedede. The Rainbow Drops extract it and reveal its form as a masked, robed being wielding a magical sword. After being defeated, it assumes its small orb form as it faces Kirby. In <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_3" title="Kirby's Dream Land 3">Kirby's Dream Land 3</a></i>, Dark Matter returns to Pop Star and possesses many of its inhabitants. After aiding various creatures in need, Kirby eventually obtains the Love-Love Stick and enters the center of the cloud known as the Hyper Zone, and defeats the Dark Matter. After its death, Kirby faces the leader of the Dark Matter, a giant white creature with a Kirby-sized red eye known as <b>Zero</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ゼロ</span><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span>.</p>
<p>The Dark Matter returns once more in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_64:_The_Crystal_Shards" title="Kirby 64: The Crystal Shards">Kirby 64: The Crystal Shards</a></i>, where they invade Ripple Star for its Crystal. When the Crystal is shattered, Kirby sets out to reassemble the pieces on five other planets before confronting a Dark Matter creature called <b>Miracle Matter</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ミラクルマター</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Mirakuru Matā</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span>. Its defeat repels the Dark Matter from Ripple Star, but the Crystal detects and expels a powerful presence of Dark Matter from the Fairy Queen, which goes on to form a new planet. In the core of this last world is <b>0²</b> (<b>Zero Two</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ゼロツー</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Zero Tsū</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span>), presumably a reincarnated version of 0 after being defeated in <i>Kirby's Dream Land 3</i>. It an angelic-looking form of Zero with a halo, geometric, segmented wings, and a green spiked tail.</p>
<p>In <i>Kirby: Squeak Squad</i>, a Dark Matter known as <b>Dark Nebula</b> (<b>Dark Zero</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ダークゼロ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Dāku Zero</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span>), is the prisoner of a treasure chest which was originally in King Dedede's possession. Meta Knight realizes what is truly inside the treasure chest and suddenly steals it to prevent his release. Kirby, thinking his cake is inside, chases him to the ruins of the Halberd under the Secret Sea. Aboard the operational Halberd, the leader of the Squeaks, Daroach, manages to open the chest and releases him. However, Dark Nebula takes over his body and escapes to Gamble Galaxy. Kirby eventually fights Daroach again and Dark Nebula is forced out. Daroach relinquishes the Triple Star, a mystical rod. With his help, Dark Nebula is banished.</p>
<p>Dark Matter makes small cameo appearances in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Squeak_Squad" title="Kirby: Squeak Squad">Kirby: Squeak Squad</a></i>, <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star_Ultra" title="Kirby Super Star Ultra">Kirby Super Star Ultra</a></i> and <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kirby:_Mass_Attack" title="Kirby: Mass Attack">Kirby: Mass Attack</a></i>. A clone of Dark Matter in its <i>Kirby's Dream Land 2</i> form, now dubbed <b>Dark Matter Clone</b>, appears as an extra boss in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Planet_Robobot" title="Kirby: Planet Robobot">Kirby: Planet Robobot</a></i>. It was created from an unknown source by the <a href="/wiki/Supercomputer" title="Supercomputer">supercomputer</a> Star Dream; however, it is noted that Star Dream was unable to fully replicate Dark Matter's powers.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Nightmare">Nightmare</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Nightmare">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Nightmare</b> (ナイトメア <i>Naitomea</i>), also known as <b>The Nightmare Wizard</b>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Melee_2-0"><a href="#cite_note-Melee-2">[2]</a></sup> is the primary antagonist and the final boss of <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Adventure" title="Kirby's Adventure">Kirby's Adventure</a></i> and its remake, <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Adventure#Remakes_and_ports" title="Kirby's Adventure">Kirby: Nightmare in Dream Land</a></i>. After Nightmare invades the miraculous Fountain of Dreams, <a href="/wiki/List_of_Kirby_characters#King_Dedede" title="List of Kirby characters">King Dedede</a> splits up the Star Rod into seven pieces and gives them to his friends, preventing Nightmare from using it to spread bad dreams. Kirby, not knowing this, finds the pieces and reunites them. Nightmare soon tries to steal it, but Kirby ends up using it to defeat him. Nightmare starts out as an orb that shoots stars, and he eventually transforms into a humanoid, vampire-like being with a tornado-like cloak for a body.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Adventure_3-0"><a href="#cite_note-Adventure-3">[3]</a></sup></p>
<p>Nightmare is also the main villain of the <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> anime. He runs <b>NightMare Enterprises</b> (ホーリーナイトメア社 <i>Hōrī Naitomea-sha</i>, <b>Holy Nightmare Company</b> in the Japanese dub) . He is given the name of <b>NME</b> in the English version. Depicted as having a more threatening persona than in the game, he is instead bent on conquering the universe, and he dominates much of the universe from the series' beginning. He uses his ability to create an endless number of creatures known as Demon Beasts (Monsters in the English dub) to conquer civilizations. He also sells them to unsuspecting customers (Like Dedede) for a profit, via a transportation network. His only opposition are the Star Warriors and Galaxy Soldier Army, though they are wiped out before the series begins. He is an embodiment of life's fear and suffering, and so he strives to bring more pain in order to increase his power, and will always exist as long as people hold fear in their hearts. In the finale, he was destroyed by Kirby using the Star Rod.</p>
<p>Nightmare is voiced by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Banjo_Ginga" title="Banjo Ginga">Banjo Ginga</a> in the Japanese version of the anime and by <a href="/wiki/Andrew_Rannells" title="Andrew Rannells">Andrew Rannells</a> in the English dub.</p>
<p>Nightmare appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Super_Smash_Bros._for_Nintendo_3DS_and_Wii_U" title="Super Smash Bros. for Nintendo 3DS and Wii U">Super Smash Bros. for Nintendo 3DS and Wii U</a></i> as an assist trophy, voiced by <a href="/wiki/Hisao_Egawa" title="Hisao Egawa">Hisao Egawa</a>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Magolor">Magolor</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Magolor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Magolor</b> appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Return_to_Dream_Land" title="Kirby's Return to Dream Land">Kirby's Return to Dream Land</a></i>, initially as a friendly character. He travels to Dream Land on an inter-dimensional ship called the <i>Lor Starcutter</i>. When the ship crash lands in Dream Land, Kirby, King Dedede, Meta Knight, and a Waddle Dee offer to help repair the <i>Lor Starcutter</i> so that he can return to a realm known as Halcandra - and as a reward for their efforts, Magolor brings Kirby and the group to Halcandra for a visit. When the group arrives, a large four-headed dragon known as Landia attacks and shoots down the Lor Starcutter for an unknown reason. Angry that they have been trapped, Magolor sends Kirby and the group to defeat Landia.</p>
<p>In truth, Magolor is a power hungry villain who is secretly using the four to defeat Landia for him, so that he could obtain the Master Crown. The Master Crown grants limitless power to the wearer, and Landia is currently in possession of this crown. Magolor wishes to become the universe's ruling overlord, but he must gain the power to do so from the Master Crown. It is revealed that Magolor had fought and lost to Landia before, and in his escape attempt he landed in Dream Land. After Landia is defeated by Kirby and the group, Magolor puts on the Master Crown and transforms into a giant floating entity with enormous power, then announces that he will conquer Pop Star as his "reward" to Kirby and his friends for their help. With help from Landia, Kirby chases Magolor into another dimension and sinks the <i>Lor Starcutter</i>, then battles Magolor himself. After his final defeat, Magolor returns to his normal self and disappears. In the Extra Mode there is an additional cinematic showing him becoming a more dark form called <b>Magolor Soul</b>, described by the game as "<i>a sad shell possessed by the limitless power of the Master Crown, no more than a manifestation of the crown itself"</i>, hinting at the possibility that Magolor may not have actually been evil but was instead corrupted by the Master Crown's power.</p>
<p>Magolor returns in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Collection" title="Kirby's Dream Collection">Kirby's Dream Collection</a></i>, revealed to be alive and reformed, where he builds Kirby a new playground. Here, Kirby can play through new challenge stages, some of which he races against Magolor. During the races, he uses magic to summon enemies, as well as attack Kirby. His rivalry with Kirby still exists, albeit more friendly.</p>
<p>After his appearance in <i>Kirby's Return to Dream Land</i>, Magolor also has made cameo appearances, usually in the form of collectables, in other games, including <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Triple_Deluxe" title="Kirby: Triple Deluxe">Kirby: Triple Deluxe</a></i>, <i>Dedede's Drum Dash Deluxe</i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Super_Smash_Bros._for_Nintendo_3DS_and_Wii_U" title="Super Smash Bros. for Nintendo 3DS and Wii U">Super Smash Bros. for Wii U</a></i>, and <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Planet_Robobot" title="Kirby: Planet Robobot">Kirby: Planet Robobot</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Marx">Marx</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Marx">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Marx</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">マルク</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Maruku</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>, Mark)</span> is the antagonist and final boss from "Milky Way Wishes" in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star</a></i> and its remake. He is a round, lavender creature, similar to Kirby, but having no arms, wearing a jester hat, a bow tie, and brown shoes. He is frequently seen bouncing on a ball.</p>
<p>In the beginning of "Milky Way Wishes", Marx tells Kirby about how the Sun and Moon are fighting and that only the power of a giant mechanical creature called Nova can make them stop, sending Kirby on the adventure. Once Nova appears, Marx suddenly pushes Kirby out of the way and wishes for control over Pop Star. Explaining that he was the one who started the fight between the Sun and Moon in the first place, Marx then turns into a more powerful form of himself, which is somewhat larger than his original form with fangs and strange yellow wings that look like two long arms with claws, before sending Nova on a collision course with Pop Star. As the Sun and Moon hold Nova back, Kirby rides a magical Starship into Nova and disables its heart, then defeats Marx and sends him crashing into Nova to destroy them both. In <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star#Remake" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star Ultra</a></i>, pieces of Nova fuse with Marx's dead body and revives him as the more powerful <b>Marx Soul</b> (マルクソウル <i>Marukusouru</i>), the final boss of the new and most difficult subgame "The True Arena" with a new design and improved attacks.</p>
<p>He makes a cameo appearance in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Squeak_Squad" title="Kirby: Squeak Squad">Kirby: Squeak Squad</a></i>, in an unlockable picture with other series villains. In <i>Super Smash Bros. Brawl</i>, an arrange of the music when Kirby is battling Marx in <i>Kirby Super Star</i> can be played on the Halberd stage. The final boss from this game, Tabuu, also shares some similar moves and pattern with Marx (both of them created by <a href="/wiki/Masahiro_Sakurai" title="Masahiro Sakurai">Masahiro Sakurai</a>) In <i>Kirby: Mass Attack</i>, he appears as the big boss of the "Kirby Brawlball" sub-game. In <i>Kirby's Return to Dream Land</i>, he makes a brief appearance in the crowd of the final Kirby Master 100% video, and if Kirby uses the Stone ability in <i>Kirby's Return to Dreamland</i>, he will occasionally turn into a stone statue of Marx in his original form bouncing on his striped ball.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dark_Mind">Dark Mind</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Dark Mind">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Dark Mind</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ダークマインド</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Dāku Maindo</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is the main villain of <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_%26_the_Amazing_Mirror" title="Kirby &amp; the Amazing Mirror">Kirby &amp; the Amazing Mirror</a></i>, with Dark Meta Knight as his right-hand man. At the intro of the game, after Meta Knight rushes into the mirror world, Dark Meta Knight slices Kirby into four, unintentionally giving Kirby backup against the corrupted Mirror World. Throughout the game, Dark Meta Knight masquerades as the real deal and a timid "Shadow Kirby" also makes its appearance. Towards the end of the game, the original Meta Knight exposes the copy during the final confrontation. After Dark Meta Knight is shattered, the way to Dark Mind is open and sucks Kirby and Meta Knight's Master Sword. After Dark Mind is defeated, it is learned that he intended to make the Mirror World be overrun with a person's worst reflection of themselves; Shadow Kirby is actually an honest reflection of the real Kirby with no such qualities, and stays behind as the guardian of the Mirror World as Meta Knight lays his Master Sword to rest.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Drawcia">Drawcia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Drawcia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Drawcia</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ドロシア</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Doroshia</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is the villain of <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Canvas_Curse" title="Kirby: Canvas Curse">Kirby: Canvas Curse</a></i>. She is an evil paint-<a href="/wiki/Witchcraft" title="Witchcraft">witch</a> and a dangerous sorceress. She curses Kirby into a ball at the start of the game and turns Pop Star into paint. She has two forms: Drawcia Sorceress and Drawcia Soul. Her first, humanoid form, can shoot balls of energy at Kirby and summon enemies to damage him (including Para Drawcias in her image) by painting them. Her second form resembles a blob of paint, and she has many paint-related techniques. When she is defeated, her curse is lifted and Pop Star and Kirby return to normal.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Yin-Yarn">Yin-Yarn</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Yin-Yarn">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Yin-Yarn</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">アミーボ・アモーレ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Amībo Amōre</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is the main villain of the Kirby game <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Epic_Yarn" title="Kirby's Epic Yarn">Kirby's Epic Yarn</a></i>. He is an evil sorcerer who wreaks chaos and havoc in Dream Land and Patch Land. When Kirby tries to eat his nose (thinking it's a tomato), Yin-Yarn traps Kirby inside a sock that sends him to Patch Land, where Kirby's body transforms into yarn. A bit later, Kirby realizes that air goes through yarn, which forces him to use the yarn whip and transformations with yarn instead. Kirby and Prince Fluff set off to recover seven pieces of yarn, defeat Yin-Yarn, and bring peace back to both Dream Land and Patch Land. Yin-Yarn is the boss of Dream Land and is fought in two forms: first, he attacks Kirby and Prince Fluff in his normal form. Secondly, he attacks them as Mega Yin-Yarn, leaving Kirby and Prince Fluff hopeless. Suddenly, Meta-Knight flies by, dropping a Tankbot Metamortex, turning them into a Tankbot to fight and defeat this evil incarnation. His name is a pun on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Yin_yang" title="Yin yang">yin yang</a>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Necrodeus">Necrodeus</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Necrodeus">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Necrodeus</b> is the primary antagonist of <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Mass_Attack" title="Kirby Mass Attack">Kirby Mass Attack</a></i>. He is the leader of a group of <a href="/wiki/Demon" title="Demon">demons</a> known as the Skull Gang. Upon appearing at the beginning of the game, Necrodeus casts a spell that splits Kirby into ten pieces, and defeats all but one Kirby. Necrodeus has the ultimate goal of shrouding Popstar in darkness, but is defeated by Kirby in the final scenes. His name means "Deathgod" in Latin, a name that accurately describes his appearance and nature. As the final boss of <i>Kirby Mass Attack</i>, he faces Kirby in two forms: first, Kirby must defeat his hands (similar to the Wham Bam Rock fight from <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star</a></i>). Upon death, Necrodeus drops his magic staff, the source of his power, which Kirby uses to restore himself to normal.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Queen_Sectonia">Queen Sectonia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Queen Sectonia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Queen Sectonia</b> is the main villain of Kirby: Triple Deluxe. She claims to be the ruler of the heavens, calling Dream Land the lower world. Sectonia ruled over her land, Floralia, with an iron fist, resulting in the people of the sky to send out the Dreamstalk, which they hope would bring Kirby, the Hero of Dream Land, to their rescue. However, Queen Sectonia sent her trusted servant, Taranza, to intercept this plan by kidnapping the Hero of Dreamland. Taranza accidentally mistakes King Dedede for Kirby and kidnaps him. Kirby then pursues Taranza in an effort to rescue Dedede. Finally, Kirby corners Taranza in Royal Road, Queen Sectonia's palace. After defeating a possessed King Dedede, Taranza calls forth Queen Sectonia in an effort to save himself, but Queen Sectonia instead shoots him, calling him a "pitiful fool." Kirby and Queen Sectonia do battle, with Kirby reigning victorious.</p>
<p>In a last ditch effort, the queen fuses herself with the Dreamstalk, with the intent of using its power to warp Popstar into her perfect vision. Kirby once again battles Sectonia, but this ends up being captured. As the queen begins to strangle Kirby, Taranza returns with King Dedede. King Dedede frees Kirby, while Taranza gives Kirby a Miracle Fruit. This allows the hero to become Hypernova Kirby. Kirby inhales Queen Sectonia's final laser blast, before spitting it back at her, killing her off for good. In the extra mode Dededetour, she is once again returns as <b>Queen Sectonia DX</b> and is fought by King Dedede.</p>
<p>She later returns in the True Arena where she consumes four Miracle Fruits turning her into <b>Soul of Sectonia</b> and once again battles Kirby. After her defeat however, she then rips herself out of the Dreamstalk to battle Kirby one last time. After her defeat she then bursts into a shower of flower petals.</p>
<p>It is hinted that she was once a gracious ruler, until she went mad over lust for beauty and vanity after Taranza brought her a magical mirror he had found in his travels. Taranza tried to convince her to reform, but was shut out by the queen.</p>
<p>A clone of Sectonia appears in <i>Kirby: Planet Robobot</i> as an extra boss, created by Star Dream using a sample from Sectonia's flower form. Some of its attacks are slightly different from her previous appearance; particularly, she now has an attack that sends jeweled shockwaves through the ground when she strikes the floor with her scepters. The clone's appearance is more zombie-like than the original Sectonia, featuring cloudy, dull eyes and broken heart patterns on its body. When defeated, the clone briefly shrinks down into a spider-like form similar to Taranza (possibly Sectonia's original form) before dying.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dark_Crafter">Dark Crafter</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Dark Crafter">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Dark Crafter</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ダーククラフター</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Dāku Kurafutā</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is the main antagonist of <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_and_the_Rainbow_Curse" title="Kirby and the Rainbow Curse">Kirby and the Rainbow Curse</a></i>. It is a creature with the strange urge to steal color from places, and possessed Claycia's body to fulfill these plans.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="President_Haltmann">President Haltmann</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: President Haltmann">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>President Max Profitt Haltmann</b> is the main antagonist of <i>Kirby: Planet Robobot</i>. As the President of Haltmann Works Company (HWC), Haltmann cares only about the prosperity of his company. To this end, he travels the galaxy in his giant spaceship, the Access Ark, and terraforms planets by stripping away their resources and converting them to giant mechanical fortresses. The plight of the natives do not interest Haltmann, whom he cruelly dismisses as "savages". At the end of the game, Kirby confronts Haltmann, who fights him in a custom-built Robobot Armor made of solid gold. After his defeat, Haltmann summons the Mother Computer, Star Dream, in his attempt to destroy Kirby, but Susie interrupts and tries to steal Star Dream. This backfires when Star Dream wakes up and uploads itself into Haltmann, possessing him and driving Star Dream to grant his wish of eternal prosperity for HWC by erasing everything else in existence. In "The True Arena", Star Dream's control over Haltmann becomes even stronger when Kirby fights its Core OS, erasing every last trace of Haltmann from its programming as Kirby disables and eventually destroys the rampaging computer.</p>
<p>In "Meta Knightmare Returns" he is faced by Meta Knight under the name <b>President Haltmann 2.0</b>, once defeated, Star Dream awakens and tests Meta Knight who it acknowledges as the new Admin</p>
<p>Pause screen descriptions in "Meta Knightmare Returns" and "The True Arena" shed additional light on Haltmann's backstory. He originally built Star Dream from ancient technology and knowledge gained from an unknown source. During an experiment with it, President Haltmann's daughter Susanna disappeared. The belief that Susanna was dead drove Haltmann insane, and he continued constructing Star Dream to grant his wish of eternal prosperity for his company. This required significant amounts of natural resources, which eventually led HWC to Pop Star.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Star_Dream">Star Dream</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Star Dream">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>A <a href="/wiki/Supercomputer" title="Supercomputer">supercomputer</a> built by the Haltmann Works Company (HWC), <b>Star Dream</b>, also known as <b>Mother Computer</b>, is the final boss of <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Planet_Robobot" title="Kirby: Planet Robobot">Kirby: Planet Robobot</a></i>. President Haltmann constructed it using ancient technology and knowledge from an unknown source. Much later, when Haltmann has been defeated by Kirby, the computer wakes up and consumes Haltmann's mind to become self-aware. Speaking through Haltmann's body, Star Dream reveals that it used the HWC and its business plan to study organic life throughout the universe. Having arrived at the conclusion that all organic life is an obstacle to prosperity and thus must be destroyed, Star Dream flies off into space and is pursued by Kirby, who has fused the Robobot Armor with the Halberd. After taking heavy damage in the ensuing dogfight, Star Dream connects itself to the HWC's mothership, the Access Ark, to continue fighting. Once the armored shell of the Access Ark is broken off, the true form of Star Dream is revealed - a Clockwork Star nearly identical to Nova, the comet used by Marx in <i>Kirby Super Star</i>. In a final battle, Kirby manages to drill completely through Star Dream, presumably destroying it.</p>
<p>In the "Meta Knightmare Returns" subgame, Star Dream requests that Meta Knight prove himself to it after Haltmann is defeated. For this purpose, it creates clones of Dark Matter and Sectonia. After these fail, it summons Galacta Knight through a space-time portal, but Galacta Knight destroys it himself before doing battle with Meta Knight.</p>
<p>In The True Arena, the damage done by Galacta Knight ends up activating a hidden program within the computer transforming it into the more powerful <b>Star Dream Soul OS</b> who is fought as the final opponent of the True Arena. Upon the defeat of its Clockwork Star form, however, the mechanical monstrosity pulls Kirby into itself. Inside, the true form of Star Dream Soul OS is revealed as an armored, mechanical heart like that of Nova. After being defeated, the heart makes one final attempt to destroy Kirby by firing immense waves of energy that can kill him on contact before finally exploding.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Supporting_characters">Supporting characters</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Supporting characters">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adeleine">Adeleine</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Adeleine">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Adeleine</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">アドレーヌ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Adorēnu</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is an artist who came to Pop Star to study art. In <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_64:_The_Crystal_Shards" title="Kirby 64: The Crystal Shards">Kirby 64: The Crystal Shards</a></i>, she appeared as one of the early boss characters taken over by Dark Matter. She is taken over and fights Kirby, and later joins with Kirby after he frees her. She has the ability to make her paintings real, either creating monsters while under the control of Dark Matter or providing Kirby with help.</p>
<p>A nearly identical character named <b>Ado</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">アド</span><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> plays a similar role in <i>Kirby's Dream Land 3</i>. It is implied that Ado and Adeleine are the same character, though there has been no confirmation.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bandana_Waddle_Dee">Bandana Waddle Dee</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Bandana Waddle Dee">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Bandana Waddle Dee</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">バンダナワドルディー</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Bandana Wadoru Dī</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span>, or <b>Bandana Dee</b> for short, is a Waddle Dee who wears a blue bandana and is frequently seen wielding a spear. He first appeared in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star</a></i> as an enemy in Megaton Punch. In the remake <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star_Ultra" title="Kirby Super Star Ultra">Kirby Super Star Ultra</a></i>, he appears in the "Revenge of the King" mode as King Dedede's minion. Bandana Waddle Dee also appears in the <i>Kirby Super Star</i><span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">'</span>s "The Arena" mode as a joke boss, which would he would reprise <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_%26_the_Amazing_Mirror" title="Kirby &amp; the Amazing Mirror">Kirby &amp; the Amazing Mirror</a></i><span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">'</span>s "Boss Endurance" mode. Beginning with <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Return_to_Dream_Land" title="Kirby's Return to Dream Land">Kirby's Return to Dream Land</a></i>, Bandana Waddle Dee transitioned into being a full-fledged protagonist and ally of Kirby, as he is one of the game's four playable characters. He also assists Kirby in both <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Triple_Deluxe" title="Kirby: Triple Deluxe">Kirby: Triple Deluxe</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Planet_Robobot" title="Kirby: Planet Robobot">Kirby: Planet Robobot</a></i> by providing him with items. In the side series, however, Bandana Waddle Dee appears as a playable character in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_and_the_Rainbow_Curse" title="Kirby and the Rainbow Curse">Kirby and the Rainbow Curse</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dyna_Blade">Dyna Blade</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Dyna Blade">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Dyna Blade</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ダイナブレイド</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Daina Bureido</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is an enormous, armored <a href="/wiki/Bird" title="Bird">bird</a> that acts as both a friend and a foe in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star</a></i>, and Kirby Super Star Ultra. In her self-titled game, she destroys all of Dream Land's crops to feed her chicks. Kirby defeats her, not knowing this, so he ends up feeding the chicks with apples and teaching them how to fly. In "Revenge of Meta Knight", Dyna Blade returns the favor by successfully carrying Kirby onto the Halberd before the artillery forces her to retreat.</p>
<p>In <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i>, Dyna Blade is shown as a legendary bird that is worshiped by the citizens of Cappytown. King Dedede hatches a plot to get rid of Kirby by tricking him into eating her egg, which infuriates Dyna Blade and causes her to chase and attack Kirby for much of the episode, until her chick appears and Kirby feeds it, placating Dyna.</p>
<p>In <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Air_Ride" title="Kirby Air Ride">Kirby Air Ride</a></i>, Dyna Blade appears in City Trial mode and sometimes flies to different parts of the city until flying away all together. The player can defeat Dyna Blade by aiming for her head to obtain multiple power ups. In <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Epic_Yarn" title="Kirby's Epic Yarn">Kirby's Epic Yarn</a></i>, a similar boss to Dyna Blade named Hot Wings appears as the boss of Hot Land.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gooey">Gooey</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Gooey">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Gooey</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">グーイ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Gūi</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a black blob with a pair of eyes and a mouth. He first appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_2" title="Kirby's Dream Land 2">Kirby's Dream Land 2</a></i> as a friend of Kirby that can be rescued from a holding bag (if Kirby is already with the animal partner that's inside it). Rescuing him at least once awards a single percentage point for 100% completion. There is also a female blob similar to Gooey that must also be rescued for 100%, though she appears more rarely.</p>
<p><i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_3" title="Kirby's Dream Land 3">Kirby's Dream Land 3</a></i> expands on Gooey's character. He is revealed to be of the Dark Matter race, but chose to be Kirby's friend instead. He can be summoned by Kirby as a helper character similar to those in <i>Kirby Super Star</i>, controlled by either the computer or a second player. Gooey's main form of offense is to snag enemies with his tongue and spit them out like Kirby does; he cannot capture multiple enemies like Kirby can, but can use his tongue underwater. Gooey can also copy abilities like Kirby, but only when a second player is controlling him. When flying in the Hyper Zone, Gooey assumes his Dark Matter form, though he still maintains his own face.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Yellow_Kirby">Yellow Kirby</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Yellow Kirby">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Yellow Kirby <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">キービィ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Kībyi</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>, often transcribed as <i>Keeby</i>)</span> is a yellow-colored Kirby whose Japanese name only officially appears in the Japanese version of <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Course" title="Kirby's Dream Course">Kirby's Dream Course</a></i>. Only playable through multiplayer mode, Yellow Kirby is Kirby's rival to see who can get the most points in a race to get to the golf hole first. Yellow Kirby also appears as an optional costume for Kirby in the <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Super_Smash_Bros._(series)" title="Super Smash Bros. (series)">Super Smash Bros. series</a></i>. In <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star#Remake" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star Ultra</a></i>, Yellow Kirby is the second player in the game "Gourmet Race", racing against Kirby. In <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Squeak_Squad" title="Kirby: Squeak Squad">Kirby: Squeak Squad</a></i>, Kirby can use spray paint to become a yellow Kirby. It is not known if Yellow Kirby in other games is supposed to be Kībī.</p>
<p>When deciding what color Kirby would be, <a href="/wiki/Shigeru_Miyamoto" title="Shigeru Miyamoto">Shigeru Miyamoto</a> wanted Kirby to be yellow. That yellow Kirby would eventually become Kībī.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Animal_Friends">Animal Friends</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Animal Friends">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_2" title="Kirby's Dream Land 2">Kirby's Dream Land 2</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_3" title="Kirby's Dream Land 3">Kirby's Dream Land 3</a></i> feature various allies that can team up with Kirby and share powers.</p>
<p><i>Kirby's Dream Land 2</i> introduces:</p>
<ul>
<li><b>Rick</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">リック</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Rikku</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> the <a href="/wiki/Hamster" title="Hamster">Hamster</a> - The most well-known helper to Kirby, Rick is able to walk on ice without slipping. In <i>Kirby's Dream Land 3</i>, Rick can also kill enemies by jumping on them and climb walls, but he is the only animal partner who cannot inhale and must walk into enemies with his mouth open in order to eat them.</li>
<li><b>Coo</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">クー</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Kū</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> the <a href="/wiki/Owl" title="Owl">Owl</a> - A wise owl that is a friend of Kirby. Coo can fly against strong winds.</li>
<li><b>Kine</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">カイン</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Kain</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> the <a href="/wiki/Molidae" title="Molidae">Ocean Sunfish</a> - Kine helps Kirby get through the water stages by being able to swim against strong currents and allowing Kirby to use his inhaling attack underwater. He is also controllable on land, albeit very slowly, and in <i>Kirby's Dream Land 3</i> can jump on foes to kill them.</li>
</ul>
<p><i>Kirby's Dream Land 3</i> introduces:</p>
<ul>
<li><b>Nago</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ナゴ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Nago</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> the <a href="/wiki/Cat" title="Cat">Cat</a> - A cat that is twice the size of Kirby. Nago can roll Kirby up into a ball and roll him around. He can also perform double or triple-jumps, and jump on foes to defeat them.</li>
<li><b>Pitch</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ピッチ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Pitchi</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> the <a href="/wiki/Bird" title="Bird">Bird</a> - He is the smallest of Kirby's animal friends. He can do powerful attacks when he has a copy ability. He can fly too, but not against strong winds.</li>
<li><b>Chuchu</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">チュチュ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Chuchu</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> the <a href="/wiki/Octopus" title="Octopus">Octopus</a> - She can be used to cling to the ceiling, but also weighs <a href="/wiki/Kirby_(character)" title="Kirby (character)">Kirby</a> down when he attempts to fly.</li>
</ul>
<p>In <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_64:_The_Crystal_Shards" title="Kirby 64: The Crystal Shards">Kirby 64: The Crystal Shards</a></i>, when Kirby uses the Cutter/Stone combo ability, he can randomly carve himself into a stone statue of his allies. Rick, Coo, and Kine also appear in the anime series <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i>. Here, Rick is shown to have an Australian accent. In <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Return_to_Dream_Land" title="Kirby's Return to Dream Land">Kirby's Return to Dream Land</a></i>, one of Stone Kirby's transformations is a statue of Rick, Coo, and Kine.</p>
<p>Rick, Coo, and Kine make a cameo in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Mass_Attack" title="Kirby Mass Attack">Kirby Mass Attack</a></i>, as the background image in the minigame "Kirby Quest". They also appear in the <i>Kirby Fighters</i> mode of <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Triple_Deluxe" title="Kirby: Triple Deluxe">Kirby: Triple Deluxe</a></i>, appearing in Coo's Forest stage where they randomly appear and attack players indiscriminately.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Prince_Fluff">Prince Fluff</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Prince Fluff">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Prince Fluff</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">フラッフ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Furaffu</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a playable character who helps Kirby in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Epic_Yarn" title="Kirby's Epic Yarn">Kirby's Epic Yarn</a></i>. He has the same abilities as Kirby. He is Kirby's size, but is blue and has larger (whiter) eyes, orange feet, and also has a golden crown on his head. He and Kirby team up to recover seven pieces of magic yarn scattered throughout the land, defeat Yin-Yarn, and bring peace back to his home, Patch Land. In 2-player mode, player 1 is Kirby and player 2 is Prince Fluff.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ribbon">Ribbon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Ribbon">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Ribbon</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">リボン</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Ribon</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a pink-haired fairy from the planet Ripple Star who appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_64:_The_Crystal_Shards" title="Kirby 64: The Crystal Shards">Kirby 64: The Crystal Shards</a></i>. She is a kind and brave character who attempted to escape her planet with the fairies' magical Crystal when it was invaded by <i><a href="/wiki/List_of_Kirby_characters#Zero_and_Dark_Matter" title="List of Kirby characters">Dark Matter</a></i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ReferenceA_4-0"><a href="#cite_note-ReferenceA-4">[4]</a></sup> In space, Dark Matter blobs ambushed her, shattered the crystal, and made her fall to Pop Star, where she lands on a stargazing Kirby and pleads with him for help.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ReferenceA_4-1"><a href="#cite_note-ReferenceA-4">[4]</a></sup> Kirby agrees and they search for the Crystal shards scattered on various planets and thwart Dark Matter's invasion of Ripple Star along with <i><a href="/wiki/List_of_Kirby_characters#Waddle_Dee" title="List of Kirby characters">Waddle Dee</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/List_of_Kirby_characters#Adeleine" title="List of Kirby characters">Adeleine</a></i>, and <i><a href="/wiki/List_of_Kirby_characters#King_Dedede" title="List of Kirby characters">King Dedede</a></i>. In the final battle, Ribbon and the crystal aid Kirby in defeating 0², the controlling force behind Dark Matter. In the ending cutscene of the game, she gives Kirby a kiss, blushing shyly afterward.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Landia">Landia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Landia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Landia</b> is a four-headed <a href="/wiki/Dragon" title="Dragon">dragon</a> from <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Return_to_Dream_Land" title="Kirby's Return to Dream Land">Kirby's Return to Dream Land</a></i>. According to the in-game description, she is an ancient guardian living in Halcandra who has protected the Master Crown and the <i>Lor Starcutter</i> since ancient times. Magolor attempted to steal the treasures she guarded, thus waking her up and forcing her into a rampage. Magolor fought against Landia himself to get it but lost, so he stole the <i>Lor Starcutter</i> and flew to Pop Star in hopes of finding someone useful to his plans. Magolor returned with Kirby, King Dedede, Meta Knight and Waddle Dee, and sicced all four on the dragon. After they defeated her, Magolor finally obtained the Master Crown and left to take over the galaxy starting with Pop Star. Landia, as four smaller dragons, helped Kirby and company in their efforts to defeat Magolor. After Magolor's defeat, Landia and the <i>Lor Starcutter</i> help Kirby and the others escape from the closing void back to Pop Star before returning home to Halcandra.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Taranza">Taranza</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Taranza">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Taranza</b> is a spider-like creature who appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Triple_Deluxe" title="Kirby: Triple Deluxe">Kirby: Triple Deluxe</a></i>. He hails from Floralia and is a retainer to Queen Sectonia. He appears to be an antagonist at first as he kidnaps King Dedede, leading Kirby to chase him up the Dreamstalk all the way to Royal Road, where he uses his hypnotic abilities to put King Dedede under his control. After Masked Dedede is defeated, he entreats Queen Sectonia to save him, but she does not: instead she strikes him with a laser beam attack, prompting Taranza to switch allegiances after this betrayal. It is hinted in the in-game descriptions that Taranza used to be friends with Queen Sectonia but recently noticed some disturbing changes in her demeanor.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Elline">Elline</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Elline">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Elline</b> is a paintbrush-like fairy who appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_and_the_Rainbow_Curse" title="Kirby and the Rainbow Curse">Kirby and the Rainbow Curse</a></i>. She helps Kirby to defeat Claycia.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Susie">Susie</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Susie">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Susie</b> appears in <i>Kirby: Planet Robobot</i> as the executive secretary of Haltmann Works Company. She is placed in charge of the project to take over Pop Star and convert it to a fully mechanized HWC planet. Kirby confronts Susie at several points, initially as a boss who fights in a custom-built Robobot Armor, and later to summon Meta Knight and King Dedede, both having been captured and experimented on during the invasion and turned into servants of HWC. In the final level, Access Ark, President Haltmann fires Susie for her repeated failures. After Kirby and Haltmann fight, Susie suddenly reveals that she's a corporate spy and attempts to steal Star Dream with the intent to sell it to the highest bidder, but Star Dream wakes up during the scuffle and begins its rampage. Susie gives Kirby a Robobot Armor and begs him to stop Star Dream, after which she escapes to unknown whereabouts.</p>
<p>In the "Meta Knightmare Returns" sub-game, new information about Susie and her relationship with Haltmann is revealed via the Pause screen. Her full name is <b>Susanna Patrya Haltmann</b>. She is implied to be President Haltmann's daughter who vanished during an experiment with Star Dream to open portals into other dimensions, only to somehow return and begin working for HWC. Despite his obsession with her, such as constructing missiles in her image and printing her face on dollar bills, Haltmann does not seem to recognize Susie or possibly refuses to.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Enemies">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Broom_Hatter">Broom Hatter</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Broom Hatter">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Broom Hatter</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ブルームハッター</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Burūmu Hattā</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a recurring enemy in the Kirby series. It has a witch-like appearance, but possesses no ranged attacks: it often walks in one direction, sweeping the floor with its broom as it goes, and sometimes changing directions should it draw near to the edge of a platform. Usually, swallowing a Broom Hatter would do nothing, but in <i>Kirby's Dream Land 3</i> they grant the Clean Ability which allows Kirby and his animal friends to attack with brooms, feather dusters, and other household tools. This ability has yet to resurface.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Chilly">Chilly</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Chilly">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Chilly</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">チリー</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Chirī</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a <a href="/wiki/Snowman" title="Snowman">snowman</a>-like monster who is a common enemy in the Kirby franchise. In the <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> episode "Dedede's Snow Job", Chilly appeared when the Ice Dragon was causing a snowfall in Cappy Town. Kirby managed to befriend Chilly. Kirby helped Chilly to fight the Ice Dragon. When the Ice Dragon was destroyed, the snow and Chilly began to melt.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Drifter">Drifter</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Drifter">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Drifter</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ドリフター</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Dorifutā</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a one-eyed <a href="/wiki/Umbrella" title="Umbrella">umbrella</a> monster that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_2" title="Kirby's Dream Land 2">Kirby's Dream Land 2</a></i>. They are often seen being held by Waddle Dee. In the <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> episode "Like Mother, Like Snail / Escargoon Rules", King Dedede buys a bulk of Drifters from Nightmare Enterprises to attack the Cappies at the time when Escargoon's mother was visiting. Kirby inhales some of the Drifters in order to become Parasol Kirby which he uses to destroy most of the Drifters.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gabon">Gabon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Gabon">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Gabon</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ガボン</span><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a skull-headed monster that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_3" title="Kirby's Dream Land 3">Kirby's Dream Land 3</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_64:_The_Crystal_Shards" title="Kirby 64: The Crystal Shards">Kirby 64: The Crystal Shards</a></i>. In the <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> episode "Scare Tactics" Pt. 2, Gabon is sent by Nightmare Enterprises to the haunted house it built to destroy Kirby. With help from Meta-Knight, Kirby became Fire Kirby and destroyed Gabon and the haunted house.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Galbo">Galbo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Galbo">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Galbo</b> is a dragon head-like enemy that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_3" title="Kirby's Dream Land 3">Kirby's Dream Land 3</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_64:_The_Crystal_Shards" title="Kirby 64: The Crystal Shards">Kirby 64: The Crystal Shards</a></i>, and <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Return_to_Dream_Land" title="Kirby's Return to Dream Land">Kirby's Return to Dream Land</a></i>. In the <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> episode "Hatch Me If You Can", Kirby finds a Galbo egg in Tokori's nest and hatches it. It turns out that Nightmare Enterprises had placed the Galbo egg under Kirby so that it would grow attached to it. Nightmare Enterprises later sent King Dedede an adult Galbo to attack Kirby with. The baby Galbo helped Kirby to fight the adult Galbo. The adult Galbo is destroyed by Fire Kirby.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gordo">Gordo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Gordo">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Gordo</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ゴルドー</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Gorudō</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a common enemy in the Kirby games. It resembles a spiked ball with two eyes. They are usually invincible, as they cannot be sucked in and in most games, none of Kirby's attacks can destroy them. They appear as part of King Dedede's Final Smash in <i>Super Smash Bros. Brawl</i>. Outside of the Kirby games, they appear as an enemy in <i><a href="/wiki/Super_Mario_Land_2:_6_Golden_Coins" title="Super Mario Land 2: 6 Golden Coins">Super Mario Land 2: 6 Golden Coins</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Knuckle_Joe">Knuckle Joe</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Knuckle Joe">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Knuckle Joe</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ナックルジョー</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Nakkuru Jō</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a fighter who utilizes a variety of punches and kicks. He appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star</a></i> and its remake as an enemy type and a helper to Kirby, and <i><a href="/wiki/Super_Smash_Bros._Brawl" title="Super Smash Bros. Brawl">Super Smash Bros. Brawl</a></i> as an Assist Trophy. After a long absence, he came back as an enemy in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Return_to_Dream_Land" title="Kirby's Return to Dream Land">Kirby's Return to Dream Land</a></i>. He also appears in <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kirby_Triple_Deluxe" title="Kirby Triple Deluxe">Kirby Triple Deluxe</a></i>, again as an enemy. He appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> as the son of a legendary Star Warrior who seeks to avenge his father's death. He attacks Kirby believing him to be the killer, though Meta Knight explains that his father was killed by his hand after he was unfortunately changed into a monster. He reappears multiple times to help Kirby.</p>
<p>He is voiced by <a href="/wiki/Minami_Takayama" title="Minami Takayama">Minami Takayama</a> in Japanese media and by <a href="/wiki/Al%C3%A9sia_Glidewell" title="Alésia Glidewell">Alésia Glidewell</a> in the English version of Brawl.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Masher">Masher</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Masher">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Masher</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">マッシャー</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Masshā</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a large flail-wielding armored monster that is an enemy in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_2" title="Kirby's Dream Land 2">Kirby's Dream Land 2</a></i>. In the <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> episode "Monster Management", Masher is one of Nightmare Enterprises' most strongest creations. Knuckle Joe (who was working as a Monster Manager at the time) had the Nightmare Enterprises Salesman send Masher to attack a weakened Kirby. Knuckle Joe then double-crosses Masher and fires an attack that Kirby swallows to become Fighter Kirby who manages to destroy Masher. In "Masher 2.0", Masher was recreated as <b>Masher 2.0</b> where he is impervious to any attack thrown at him and now sports a larger flail and mechanical wings. It attacked Knuckle Joe with some Generic Monsters causing Knuckle Joe to flee to Dream Land. With help from Knuckle Joe and Meta-Knight, Fighter Kirby was able to destroy Masher 2.0.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mumbies">Mumbies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Mumbies">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Mumbies</b> is a <a href="/wiki/Mummy" title="Mummy">mummy</a> ball that appeared in most of the games in the Kirby franchise. They are balls covered in bandages and are usually able to resist Kirby's inhaling.</p>
<p>In the <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> episode "Mumbies Madness", King Dedede tricked Curio into digging up a jar containing Mumbies.
