When Curio released them from their jar, Mumbies went around Cappy Town scaring everyone. Mumbies even attacked Kirby where it's true mission was to target Star Warriors. Eventually, Bomb Kirby was able to trick Mumbies into clamping onto him with its teeth without letting go until the sun came out at which point the sunlight burnt Mumbies to a crisp.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noddy">Noddy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Noddy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Noddy</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ノディ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Nodi</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a common enemy in the Kirby franchise. It is a round sleeping enemy which, if inhaled by Kirby, transforms him into Sleep Kirby. This ability is useless, as all it does is make Kirby sleep for a few seconds before he wakes up and it vanishes.</p>
<p>In the <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya">Kirby: Right Back at Ya</a></i> episode "The Pillow Case", there were Noddies in the pillowcases that the Cappies purchased from King Dedede which induced nightmares revolving around Kirby. The pillows were destroyed by Meta-Knight and the Noddies end up running. In "Flower Power", King Dedede tricks Kirby into inhaling a Noddy which causes Kirby to fall asleep. Tiff, Tuff, Meta Knight, Fololo and Falala set out to find the Pukey Flower to wake him up. It's said that eating Noddy would force Kirby to sleep for about 100 years (as opposed to the five or so seconds in the video games).</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Popon">Popon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Popon">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Popon</b> is a towering enemy made up of green balls that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_3" title="Kirby's Dream Land 3">Kirby's Dream Land 3</a></i>. In the <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> episode "The Big Taste Test", Popon took on the disguise of Chef Kawasaki's teacher Chef Shiitake. When Popon's ruse was expose, Popon removed his disguise and went on the attack. Popon was destroyed by Cook Kirby.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sasuke">Sasuke</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Sasuke">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Sasuke</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">サスケ</span><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a common enemy in the Kirby franchise. In the <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> episode "Cappy New Year", King Dedede orders Sasuke from Nightmare Enterprises. He is an expert with firearms and explosives. Sasuke is destroyed when Kirby inhales him for his parasol ability.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Scarfy">Scarfy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Scarfy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Scarfy</b> is a recurring enemy in the Kirby series. It resembles a large orange ball with pointy ears. When Kirby tries to inhale Scarfy, it transforms into a biege-colored, ghastly, one-eyed version of itself called <b>Mutant Scarfy</b> which will follow Kirby and then explode. In <i>Kirby Super Star</i>, attacking a Scarfy with enough force will cause it to explode instantly. In games before this, any attack other than inhaling will trigger this reaction.</p>
<p>In the <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> episode "Dedede's Pet Threat", King Dedede buys four Scarfys from Nightmare Enterprises. Their appetites made King Dedede bankrupt and he ended up releasing the Scarfies. While in the wild, the Scarfys started eating the animals and reproducing. The Scarfys then ate the bones given to them by Nightmare Enterprises which gave them the ability to assume their mutated form. This caused a Scarfy army to form overnight that only Hammer Kirby could stop. Yet King Dedede was forced to keep the Scarfys.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Squishy">Squishy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Squishy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Squishy</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">スクイッシー</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Sukuisshī</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a <a href="/wiki/Squid" title="Squid">squid</a>-like enemy that appeared in the Kirby franchise. In the <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> episode "Dedede's Raw Deal", a smaller Squishy was seen as part of King Dedede's sushi shop plot which gave Kirby hiccups. When Kirby is unable to eat the Squishy, it grew to <a href="/wiki/Kraken" title="Kraken">Kraken</a> size where it had electrical attacks (which Master Green has). Tiff was able to scare the hiccups out of Kirby as he inhales some of Squishy's sparks to become Spark Kirby who destroys Squishy.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Waddle_Dee">Waddle Dee</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Waddle Dee">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Waddle Dee</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ワドルディー</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Wadoru Dī</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> are primarily red/tan creatures that have a somewhat similar appearance to Kirby. Waddle Dee, along with their Waddle Doo counterpart, first appeared in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land" title="Kirby's Dream Land">Kirby's Dream Land</a></i> and has since then appeared in every Kirby game to date. In <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star</a></i> during the "Revenge of Meta Knight" mode, a Waddle Dee wearing a sailor hat (often named "Sailor Waddle Dee") is part of Meta Knight's crew on the Halberd. However, he is never seen outside of enemy conversation however.</p>
<p>In <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_64:_The_Crystal_Shards" title="Kirby 64: The Crystal Shards">Kirby 64: The Crystal Shards</a></i>, one Waddle Dee, in contrast to his usual role as a common enemy, helps Kirby in his adventure. Waddle Dee is, at first, possessed by <a href="/wiki/List_of_Kirby_characters#Zero_and_Dark_Matter" title="List of Kirby characters">Dark Matter</a>, transformed into a Waddle Doo, and forced to engage Kirby. After defeating him, Waddle Dee returns to his peaceful self and catches up with Kirby to join his group alongside <a href="/wiki/List_of_Kirby_characters#Ribbon" title="List of Kirby characters">Ribbon</a>. An average Waddle Dee also appears as a playable character in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Canvas_Curse" title="Kirby: Canvas Curse">Kirby: Canvas Curse</a></i>.</p>
<p>Multiple Waddle Dees appear in <i><a href="/wiki/Super_Smash_Bros._Brawl" title="Super Smash Bros. Brawl">Super Smash Bros. Brawl</a></i>, along with Waddle Doos and Gordos, as part of King Dedede's "weapons", summoned through his side special move by being pulled from his left sleeve or by using his Final Smash, Waddle Dee Army. There are also many types of Waddle Dee such as Parasol Waddle Dee (which gives the ability), Fluff Waddle Dee, Cart Waddle Dee, Spear Waddle Dee, Swinging Waddle Dee, Balloon Waddle Dee, Big Waddle Dee, Golden Waddle Dee, and Buggie Dee. Waddle Dee have been seen to be in other colors besides red, such as yellow (in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star#Remake" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star Ultra</a></i> "Helper to Hero" mode), gold, and purple (In the "Milky Way Wishes" mode of <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star</a></i> and its sequel). In <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Epic_Yarn" title="Kirby's Epic Yarn">Kirby's Epic Yarn</a></i>, Yarn Waddle Dees, created by the sorcerer Yin Yarn, appear, but do not hurt Kirby unless carrying a weapon, such as a spear, or bow and arrow. There are also Balloon Waddle Dees, floating from a bunch of balloons that Kirby can ride on, but the balloons eventually deflate. In <i>Kirby's Avalanche</i>, Waddle Dee replaces Skeleton T as the player's opponent in the first lesson.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Waddle_Doo">Waddle Doo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Waddle Doo">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Waddle Doo</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ワドルドゥー</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Wadoru Do~ū</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a cyclops creature with an orange body, stubby arms, and purple shoes. It has a giant eyeball for a face. It shoots beams and, in the anime appearance, has a small dagger for a weapon (though he never uses it). In the anime, he is King Dedede's right-hand man as the leader of Waddle Dee troops and gives orders under King Dedede's commands. If swallowed by Kirby in most Kirby games, Kirby is given the Beam Ability and is able to shoot powerful beams at foes. Waddle Doo first appeared in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land" title="Kirby's Dream Land">Kirby's Dream Land</a></i>, and has since then been consistent in his appearance in Kirby games. In <i>Kirby 64</i>, Waddle Doo only appeared as a version of Waddle Dee possessed by <a href="/wiki/List_of_Kirby_characters#Zero_and_Dark_Matter" title="List of Kirby characters">Dark Matter</a>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Walky">Walky</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Walky">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Walky</b> is a walking <a href="/wiki/Microphone" title="Microphone">microphone</a> that is a recurring enemy in the Kirby franchise. Kirby would inhale it in order to become Mike Kirby. In the <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> episode "Abusement Park", King Dedede ordered a Walky from Nightmare Enterprises where it was used in King Dedede's karaoke contest where Kirby would perform on the teleporter that would take him to Nightmare Enterprises and be attacked by the waiting monsters. When Kirby inhaled Walky and became Mike Kirby, he was teleported to Nightmare Enterprises where his singing destroyed the waiting monsters and caused the Nightmare Enterprises Salesman to send him as Kirby's singing ended up leveling Castle Dedede. In the end, Kirby wants to sing again, but Walky (who apparently survived the inhalation) has had enough and runs away.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Mini-Bosses">Mini-Bosses</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Mini-Bosses">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The following are mini-bosses in the Kirby franchise. When a boss is defeated, Kirby can inhale them for the ability that they possess.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Batafire">Batafire</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: Batafire">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Batafire</b> (also called <b>Fire Bat</b>) is a fiery <a href="/wiki/Bat" title="Bat">bat</a> that is the mini-boss of <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_%26_the_Amazing_Mirror" title="Kirby &amp; the Amazing Mirror">Kirby &amp; the Amazing Mirror</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Big_Birdee">Big Birdee</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: Big Birdee">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Big Birdee</b> is a mini-boss that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Mass_Attack" title="Kirby Mass Attack">Kirby Mass Attack</a></i> who is encountered in Green Grounds. When encountered later again in Sandy Valley, Kirby saves the Wee Birdees from the Gegs and Big Birdee becomes an ally to Kirby for the rest of the game.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Big_Metalun">Big Metalun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Big Metalun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Big Metalun</b> is a large one-eyed Metalun that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Squeak_Squad" title="Kirby: Squeak Squad">Kirby: Squeak Squad</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Big_Warwiggle">Big Warwiggle</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Big Warwiggle">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Big Warwiggle</b> is a large Warwiggle that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Mass_Attack" title="Kirby Mass Attack">Kirby Mass Attack</a></i>. He first appears in Green Grounds and later appears in Volcano Valley.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Blast_Mariner">Blast Mariner</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=54" title="Edit section: Blast Mariner">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Blast Mariner</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ヘーチョー</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Hēchō</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a large Cannon Mariner that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Epic_Yarn" title="Kirby's Epic Yarn">Kirby's Epic Yarn</a></i>. He is the mini-boss of Water Land's Boom Boatyard.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Blocky">Blocky</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=55" title="Edit section: Blocky">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Blocky</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ブロッキー</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Burokkī</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a walking <a href="/wiki/Rock_(geology)" title="Rock (geology)">stone</a> cube that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_2" title="Kirby's Dream Land 2">Kirby's Dream Land 2</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_3" title="Kirby's Dream Land 3">Kirby's Dream Land 3</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Mass_Attack" title="Kirby Mass Attack">Kirby Mass Attack</a></i>, and <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Triple_Deluxe" title="Kirby: Triple Deluxe">Kirby: Triple Deluxe</a></i> as a mini-boss. In the <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> episode "A Blockbuster Battle", King Dedede orders Blocky from Nightmare Enterprises and sends it to attack Kirby at the time when Tiff and Tuff are finding him a place to live. Kirby defeats it as Stone Kirby where Blocky sinks to the bottom of the ocean.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Boboo">Boboo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=56" title="Edit section: Boboo">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Boboo</b> is a large Bobo that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_3" title="Kirby's Dream Land 3">Kirby's Dream Land 3</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bombar">Bombar</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=57" title="Edit section: Bombar">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Bombar</b> is a living <a href="/wiki/Fighter_aircraft" title="Fighter aircraft">jet</a> who is a rare mini-boss in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_%26_the_Amazing_Mirror" title="Kirby &amp; the Amazing Mirror">Kirby &amp; the Amazing Mirror</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bonkers">Bonkers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=58" title="Edit section: Bonkers">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Bonkers</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ボンカース</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Bonkāsu</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is an armored hammer-wielding <a href="/wiki/Gorilla" title="Gorilla">gorilla</a>-like mini-boss that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Adventure" title="Kirby's Adventure">Kirby's Adventure</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Triple_Deluxe" title="Kirby: Triple Deluxe">Kirby: Triple Deluxe</a></i> and in other Kirby games. In the <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> episode "Goin' Bonkers", Bonkers is depicted as having lived in the jungle until he was captured by a <a href="/wiki/Circus" title="Circus">circus</a> for their act. Upon watching Kirby's show, Bonkers escapes from the circus and travels to Dream Land to train with Kirby. King Dedede later has Nightmare Enterprises transform Bonkers into a monster where it ends up capturing Tiff and climbing to the top of Castle Dedede. Kirby became Hammer Kirby and managed to defeat Bonkers enough to restore him to normal. Bonkers then leaves Dream Land to continue his training.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Box_Boxer">Box Boxer</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=59" title="Edit section: Box Boxer">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Box Boxer</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">バウ・ファイター</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Bau Faitā</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a <a href="/wiki/Dog" title="Dog">dog</a> head with long arm-like ears and two feet that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_%26_the_Amazing_Mirror" title="Kirby &amp; the Amazing Mirror">Kirby &amp; the Amazing Mirror</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Squeak_Squad" title="Kirby: Squeak Squad">Kirby: Squeak Squad</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Boxy">Boxy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: Boxy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Boxy</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ボクシィ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Bokushī</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a <a href="/wiki/Box" title="Box">box</a>-like enemy that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_%26_the_Amazing_Mirror" title="Kirby &amp; the Amazing Mirror">Kirby &amp; the Amazing Mirror</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Squeak_Squad" title="Kirby: Squeak Squad">Kirby: Squeak Squad</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Buboo">Buboo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=61" title="Edit section: Buboo">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Buboo</b> is a bubble-covered creature that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Squeak_Squad" title="Kirby: Squeak Squad">Kirby: Squeak Squad</a></i>. When enough damage has been taken, Buboo's true form is a small <a href="/wiki/Crab" title="Crab">crab</a>-like creature.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bugzzy">Bugzzy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=62" title="Edit section: Bugzzy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Bugzzy</b> is a humanoid <a href="/wiki/Stag_beetle" title="Stag beetle">stag beetle</a> who is a recurring mini-boss in the Kirby franchise. He would use his mandibles to pick up and throw whatever it grabs. In the <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> episode "Kirby's Duel Role", King Dedede discovers that Kirby isn't good in a sword duel with Meta-Knight and orders a monster from Nightmare Enterprises that is capable of using a sword. Nightmare Enterprises sends over Bugzzy (who is depicted in the anime to wield a sword and a large club) as King Dedede unleashes it upon Kirby. With help from Meta-Knight, Kirby becomes Sword Kirby and slices Bugzzy in half.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hamsturr">Hamsturr</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=63" title="Edit section: Hamsturr">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Hamsturr</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ブルハンマー</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Buruhanmā</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is an animatronic <a href="/wiki/Mouse" title="Mouse">mouse</a>/<a href="/wiki/Dog" title="Dog">dog</a> enemy that wields a flail and shield who appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Mass_Attack" title="Kirby Mass Attack">Kirby Mass Attack</a></i>. He is the mini-boss of Dedede Resort.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Buzzybat">Buzzybat</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=64" title="Edit section: Buzzybat">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Buzzybat</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">バズ・バット</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Bazu Batto</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a yellow <a href="/wiki/Bat" title="Bat">bat</a> who appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Mass_Attack" title="Kirby Mass Attack">Kirby Mass Attack</a></i>. Kirby encounters Buzzy Bat in Volcano Valley. In its normal form, Buzzy Bat looks like a yellow bat with large round eyes and small purple wings. In his grave form, <b>Grave Form</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">モノ・グレイブ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Mono Gureibu</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> he resembles a flying tombstone with one eye and small wings.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Captain_Stitch">Captain Stitch</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=65" title="Edit section: Captain Stitch">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Captain Stitch</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">キャプテンステッチ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Kyaputen Sutetchi</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a spiked ball that resembles a much larger Gordo, except he's defeatable when not covered in spikes. He appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_2" title="Kirby's Dream Land 2">Kirby's Dream Land 2</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_3" title="Kirby's Dream Land 3">Kirby's Dream Land 3</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Chef_Kawasaki">Chef Kawasaki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=66" title="Edit section: Chef Kawasaki">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b><a href="/wiki/Chef" title="Chef">Chef</a> Kawasaki</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">コックカワサキ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Kokku Kawasaki</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>, Cook Kawasaki)</span>, also known as Cook Kawasaki, is an enemy that first appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star#Remake" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star Ultra</a></i>. He throws dishes and uses a frying pan that extends in an attempt to catch and fry Kirby for damage. He gives Kirby the Cook ability which is also used in <i><a href="/wiki/Super_Smash_Bros._Brawl" title="Super Smash Bros. Brawl">Super Smash Bros. Brawl</a></i> as Kirby's Final Smash. However, he appears as a friendly character in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_3" title="Kirby's Dream Land 3">Kirby's Dream Land 3</a></i>, where he plays a game with Kirby.</p>
<p>He also appears in the anime <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> where he runs the only restaurant in Cappytown. He is voiced by <a href="/wiki/Nobuo_Tobita" title="Nobuo Tobita">Nobuo Tobita</a> in the Japanese version and by the late <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Madeleine_Blaustein" title="Madeleine Blaustein">Madeleine Blaustein</a> in the English dub.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dubior">Dubior</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=67" title="Edit section: Dubior">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Dubior</b> is a <a href="/wiki/Unidentified_flying_object" title="Unidentified flying object">UFO</a>-like <a href="/wiki/Robot" title="Robot">robot</a> that appears in <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Return_to_Dreamland" title="Kirby's Return to Dreamland">Kirby's Return to Dreamland</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Planet_Robobot" title="Kirby: Planet Robobot">Kirby: Planet Robobot</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Efreeti">Efreeti</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=68" title="Edit section: Efreeti">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Efreeti</b> is a black <a href="/wiki/Hedgehog" title="Hedgehog">hedgehog</a>-like creature that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_2" title="Kirby's Dream Land 2">Kirby's Dream Land 2</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fire_Lion">Fire Lion</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=69" title="Edit section: Fire Lion">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Fire Lion</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ファイアーライオン</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Faiā Raion</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a <a href="/wiki/Lion" title="Lion">lion</a> with a fiery mane that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Adventure" title="Kirby's Adventure">Kirby's Adventure</a></i> and <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star_Ultra" title="Kirby Super Star Ultra">Kirby Super Star Ultra</a></i> in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star#DS_Exclusive_modes" title="Kirby Super Star">Revenge of the King</a></i>. In the <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> episode "Junk Jam", Fire Lion is depicted as a fiery lion. When Nightmare Enterprises refuses to stop dumping garbage on Cappy Town until King Dedede pays his bills, King Dedede and Escargoon hack into Nightmare Enterprise's computer and use it to summon Fire Lion to burn all the trash in town. Yet King Dedede couldn't control the Fire Lion and it went on a rampage. Kirby became Fire Kirby and overpowered Fire Lion enough to launch him into the ocean which destroyed Fire Lion.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Freezy_Rex">Freezy Rex</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=70" title="Edit section: Freezy Rex">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Freezy Rex</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ブリザルドン</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Burizarudon</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a large-chinned ice <a href="/wiki/Tyrannosaurus" title="Tyrannosaurus">Tyrannosaurus</a> that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Mass_Attack" title="Kirby Mass Attack">Kirby Mass Attack</a></i>. He is the mini-boss of Dedede Resort. Besides using ice attacks, Freezy Rex's chin is known to smash Gordos.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gao_Gao">Gao Gao</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=71" title="Edit section: Gao Gao">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Gao Gao</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ガオガオ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Gao Gao</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a blue <a href="/wiki/Dog" title="Dog">dog</a>-like mini-boss that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Squeak_Squad" title="Kirby: Squeak Squad">Kirby: Squeak Squad</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Giant_Stactus">Giant Stactus</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=72" title="Edit section: Giant Stactus">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Giant Stactus</b> is a large Stactus that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Mass_Attack" title="Kirby Mass Attack">Kirby Mass Attack</a></i>. He is the mini-boss of Sandy Canyon.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Giga_Clanksprout">Giga Clanksprout</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=73" title="Edit section: Giga Clanksprout">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Giga Clanksprout</b> is a large Clanksprout that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Mass_Attack" title="Kirby Mass Attack">Kirby Mass Attack</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gigant_Edge">Gigant Edge</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=74" title="Edit section: Gigant Edge">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Gigant Edge</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ギガントエッジ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Giganto Ejji</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a large <a href="/wiki/Knight" title="Knight">knight</a> in green and teal armor that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Return_to_Dream_Land" title="Kirby's Return to Dream Land">Kirby's Return to Dream Land</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Triple_Deluxe" title="Kirby: Triple Deluxe">Kirby: Triple Deluxe</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Grand_Wheelie">Grand Wheelie</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=75" title="Edit section: Grand Wheelie">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Grand Wheelie</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">グランドウイリー</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Gurando Uirī</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a giant Wheelie that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Adventure" title="Kirby's Adventure">Kirby's Adventure</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Triple_Deluxe" title="Kirby: Triple Deluxe">Kirby: Triple Deluxe</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Great_Gear">Great Gear</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=76" title="Edit section: Great Gear">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Great Gear</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">グルギアント</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Gurugianto</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a giant gear-like monster that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Mass_Attack" title="Kirby Mass Attack">Kirby Mass Attack</a></i>. He is the mini-boss of Sandy Canyon and later appears in Volcano Valley.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Haboki">Haboki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=77" title="Edit section: Haboki">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Haboki</b> is a giant <a href="/wiki/Broom" title="Broom">broom</a> monster that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_3" title="Kirby's Dream Land 3">Kirby's Dream Land 3</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Iron_Mam">Iron Mam</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=78" title="Edit section: Iron Mam">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Iron Mam</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">アイアンマム</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Aian Mamu</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is an armored baby that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Jukid">Jukid</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=79" title="Edit section: Jukid">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Jukid</b> is an inexperienced martial artist that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star</a></i>. In the <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> episode "Cowardly Creature", Jukid is among the creatures at Nightmare Enterprise's training school.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Jumpershoot">Jumpershoot</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=80" title="Edit section: Jumpershoot">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Jumpershoot</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ジャンパーシュート</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Janpāshūto</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a <a href="/wiki/Kasa-obake" title="Kasa-obake">Kasa-obake</a> that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_2" title="Kirby's Dream Land 2">Kirby's Dream Land 2</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_3" title="Kirby's Dream Land 3">Kirby's Dream Land 3</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Kibble_Blade">Kibble Blade</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=81" title="Edit section: Kibble Blade">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Kibble Blade</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ザンキブル</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Zankiburu</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a larger version of Sir Kibble that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Return_to_Dream_Land" title="Kirby's Return to Dream Land">Kirby's Return to Dream Land</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="King_Doo">King Doo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=82" title="Edit section: King Doo">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>King Doo</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">キングス・ドゥ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Kingusu Dū</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a large Waddle Doo that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Return_to_Dream_Land" title="Kirby's Return to Dream Land">Kirby's Return to Dream Land</a></i>. He is the mini-boss of Raisin Ruins.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="King_Eelongo">King Eelongo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=83" title="Edit section: King Eelongo">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>King Eelongo</b> is a brown titanic stone Eelongo that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Mass_Attack" title="Kirby Mass Attack">Kirby Mass Attack</a></i>. He is the mini-boss of Dedede Resort.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Kracko_Jr.">Kracko Jr.</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=84" title="Edit section: Kracko Jr.">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Kracko Jr.</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">クラッコジュニア</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Kurakko Junia</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a half-cloud with an eyeball in its center and rotating cloud dots who first appeared in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land" title="Kirby's Dream Land">Kirby's Dream Land</a></i> as a mini-boss. It usually drops Waddle Doos and bombs at Kirby. When defeated, it turns into its more recognized form of Kracko.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Master_Green">Master Green</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=85" title="Edit section: Master Green">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Master Green</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">マスターグリーン</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Masutā Gurīn</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a large <a href="/wiki/Jellyfish" title="Jellyfish">jellyfish</a>-like monster that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_2" title="Kirby's Dream Land 2">Kirby's Dream Land 2</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Master_Hand">Master Hand</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=86" title="Edit section: Master Hand">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Master Hand</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">マスターハンド</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Masutā Hando</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a giant right hand that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_%26_the_Amazing_Mirror" title="Kirby &amp; the Amazing Mirror">Kirby &amp; the Amazing Mirror</a></i>. It fights Kirby solo as a mini-boss, but is joined by a giant left hand named <b>Crazy Hand</b> as the dual guardians of a Mirror Shard. Master Hand's appearance and the ability it gives Kirby (Smash) is a reference to HAL's <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Super_Smash_Bros._(series)" title="Super Smash Bros. (series)">Super Smash Bros.</a></i> series.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Megatank">Megatank</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=87" title="Edit section: Megatank">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Megatank</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">クアドガン</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Kuadogan</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a large <a href="/wiki/Tank" title="Tank">tank</a>-like machine with four eyes that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Mass_Attack" title="Kirby Mass Attack">Kirby Mass Attack</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Miasmeros">Miasmeros</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=88" title="Edit section: Miasmeros">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Miasmeros</b> is a giant blob of poisonous sludge with various debris sticking out of its back, appearing in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Planet_Robobot" title="Kirby: Planet Robobot">Kirby: Planet Robobot</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Moley">Moley</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=89" title="Edit section: Moley">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Moley</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">モーリィ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Mōrī</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a large mole that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_%26_the_Amazing_Mirror" title="Kirby &amp; the Amazing Mirror">Kirby &amp; the Amazing Mirror</a></i>. He is the boss of Cabbage Cavern. He also appears in Kirby Mass Attack as a miniboss.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Moundo">Moundo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=90" title="Edit section: Moundo">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Moundo</b> is a large brown rock monster that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Return_to_Dream_Land" title="Kirby's Return to Dream Land">Kirby's Return to Dream Land</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mr._Frosty">Mr. Frosty</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=91" title="Edit section: Mr. Frosty">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Mr. Frosty</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ミスターフロスティ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Misutā Furosuti</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a humanoid tuskless <a href="/wiki/Walrus" title="Walrus">walrus</a> monster that is a recurring mini-boss in the Kirby franchise. In the <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> episode "Cowardly Creature", Mr. Frosty makes a cameo at Nightmare Enterprise's Monster Training School.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mr._Tick_Tock">Mr. Tick Tock</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=92" title="Edit section: Mr. Tick Tock">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Mr. Tick Tock</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ミスター・チクタク</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Misutā Chikku Takku</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is an anthropomorphic <a href="/wiki/Alarm_clock" title="Alarm clock">alarm clock</a> that first appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Adventure" title="Kirby's Adventure">Kirby's Adventure</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Phan_Phan">Phan Phan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=93" title="Edit section: Phan Phan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Phan Phan</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ファンファン</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Fan Fan</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is an <a href="/wiki/Elephant" title="Elephant">elephant</a> head with two legs that is a recurring mini-boss in the Kirby franchise starting with <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kirby:_Nightmare_in_Dream_Land" title="Kirby: Nightmare in Dream Land">Kirby: Nightmare in Dream Land</a></i> (where Phan Phan replaced a creature known as Rolling Turtle).</p>
<p>In the <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> episode "Cowardly Creature", Phan Phan was a student at Nightmare Enterprises' Monster Training School where it escaped and landed in Cappy Town. The Nightmare Enterprises Salesman enlisted King Dedede to help recapture Phan Phan. Upon receiving the training Monster Whippy, King Dedede got control over Phan Phan and used it to attack Kirby. After Throw Kirby managed to defeat Whippy, Phan Phan returned to normal. In "Cappy Town Down," Phan Phan was seen in Whispy Woods Forest watching the ignition of the Halberd with Whispy Woods and the other wildlife that lives there.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Rolling_Turtle">Rolling Turtle</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=94" title="Edit section: Rolling Turtle">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Rolling Turtle</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ローリングタートル</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Rōringu Tātoru</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a <a href="/wiki/Turtle" title="Turtle">turtle</a>-like monster that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Adventure" title="Kirby's Adventure">Kirby's Adventure</a></i>. He is later replaced by Phan Phan in the remake of this game, <i>Kirby: Nightmare in Dream Land</i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Shadowbite">Shadowbite</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=95" title="Edit section: Shadowbite">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Shadowbite</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">シャドーバイト</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Shadōbaito</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a <a href="/wiki/Dinosaur" title="Dinosaur">dinosaur</a> head shadow that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Mass_Attack" title="Kirby Mass Attack">Kirby Mass Attack</a></i>. He is a mini-boss in Volcano Valley.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Skullseer">Skullseer</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=96" title="Edit section: Skullseer">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Skullseer</b> is a giant Skully that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Mass_Attack" title="Kirby Mass Attack">Kirby Mass Attack</a></i>. He is the leader of the Skullys that were created by Necrodeus and is the mini-boss of Volcano Valley.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Space_Kracko">Space Kracko</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=97" title="Edit section: Space Kracko">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Space Kracko</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">スペースクラッコ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Supēsu Kurakko</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a black version of Kracko that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Epic_Yarn" title="Kirby's Epic Yarn">Kirby's Epic Yarn</a></i>. He is the mini-boss of Space Land's Outer Rings.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Space_Oohroo_Spaceship">Space Oohroo Spaceship</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=98" title="Edit section: Space Oohroo Spaceship">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Space Oohroo Spaceship</b> is a spaceship controlled by Space Oohroo that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Mass_Attack" title="Kirby Mass Attack">Kirby Mass Attack</a></i>. It is the mini-boss of Volcano Valley.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sphere_Doomer">Sphere Doomer</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=99" title="Edit section: Sphere Doomer">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Sphere Doomer</b> are Doomers that appear in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Return_to_Dream_Land" title="Kirby's Return to Dream Land">Kirby's Return to Dream Land</a></i> and come in different types.</p>
<ul>
<li><b>Regular Sphere Doomer</b> - The Regular Sphere Doomers are encountered in Cookie Country and Dangerous Dinner.</li>
<li><b>Fire Sphere Doomer</b> - The Fire Sphere Doomers are encountered in Raisin Ruins, Onion Ocean, and Dangerous Dinner.</li>
<li><b>Spark Sphere Doomer</b> - The Spark Sphere Doomers are encountered in White Wafers and Nutty Noon.</li>
<li><b>Ice Sphere Doomer</b> - The Ice Sphere Doomers are encountered in Egg Engines and Dangerous Dinner.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Star_Block_Waddle_Dee">Star Block Waddle Dee</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=100" title="Edit section: Star Block Waddle Dee">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Star Block Waddle Dee</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ブロックワドルディー</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Burokku Wadoru Dī</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a Waddle Dee in a Star Block that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Mass_Attack" title="Kirby Mass Attack">Kirby Mass Attack</a></i>. It is the mini-boss of Dedede Resort.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Steelsnapper">Steelsnapper</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=101" title="Edit section: Steelsnapper">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Steelsnapper</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">アイアン・ジャム</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Aian Jamu</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a mechanical <a href="/wiki/Eel" title="Eel">eel</a> that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Mass_Attack" title="Kirby Mass Attack">Kirby Mass Attack</a></i>. It is the mini-boss of Dedede Resort.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Super_Bonkers">Super Bonkers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=102" title="Edit section: Super Bonkers">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Super Bonkers</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">スーパー・ボンカース</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Sūpā Bonkāsu</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a powerful version of Bonkers that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Return_to_Dream_Land" title="Kirby's Return to Dream Land">Kirby's Return to Dream Land</a></i>. He sports a purple-maroon armor coat and is more aggressive than Bonkers.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tedhaun">Tedhaun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=103" title="Edit section: Tedhaun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Tedhaun</b> is a one-eyed <a href="/wiki/Ghost" title="Ghost">ghost</a> in a wizard hat that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Squeak_Squad" title="Kirby: Squeak Squad">Kirby: Squeak Squad</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Telepathos">Telepathos</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=104" title="Edit section: Telepathos">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Telepathos</b> is a horned head with two disembodied hands that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Planet_Robobot" title="Kirby: Planet Robobot">Kirby: Planet Robobot</a></i>. It uses a variety of psychic powers to attack Kirby.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tortletummy">Tortletummy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=105" title="Edit section: Tortletummy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Tortletummy</b> is a massive green <a href="/wiki/Turtle" title="Turtle">turtle</a> that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Mass_Attack" title="Kirby Mass Attack">Kirby Mass Attack</a></i>. He is the mini-boss of Green Grounds and Dedede Resort.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Waiu">Waiu</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=106" title="Edit section: Waiu">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Waiu</b> is a humanoid <a href="/wiki/Ninja" title="Ninja">ninja</a> that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_2" title="Kirby's Dream Land 2">Kirby's Dream Land 2</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Water_Galboros">Water Galboros</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=107" title="Edit section: Water Galboros">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Water Galboros</b> is a larger version of Water Galbo that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Return_to_Dream_Land" title="Kirby's Return to Dream Land">Kirby's Return to Dream Land</a></i>. In <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Triple_Deluxe" title="Kirby: Triple Deluxe">Kirby: Triple Deluxe</a></i>, a fiery version called Flame Galboros appears and gives you the fire ability instead of water.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wicked_Willow">Wicked Willow</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=108" title="Edit section: Wicked Willow">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Wicked Willow</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">トーセンボク</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Tōsenboku</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a ghastly <a href="/wiki/Tree" title="Tree">tree</a> that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Epic_Yarn" title="Kirby's Epic Yarn">Kirby's Epic Yarn</a></i>. It is the mini-boss of Grass Land's Weird Woods.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Yuki">Yuki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=109" title="Edit section: Yuki">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Yuki</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ユキ</span><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a <a href="/wiki/Snowman" title="Snowman">snowman</a>-like monster that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_3" title="Kirby's Dream Land 3">Kirby's Dream Land 3</a></i>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Bosses">Bosses</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=110" title="Edit section: Bosses">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Acro">Acro</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=111" title="Edit section: Acro">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Acro</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">アクロ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Akuro</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a <a href="/wiki/Killer_whale" title="Killer whale">killer whale</a> that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_3" title="Kirby's Dream Land 3">Kirby's Dream Land 3</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_64:_The_Crystal_Shards" title="Kirby 64: The Crystal Shards">Kirby 64: The Crystal Shards</a></i>. His name is "orca" spelled backwards. In <i>Kirby's Dream Land 3</i>, Acro is the boss of Ripple Field where it was disturbed by King Dedede. In <i>Kirby 64: The Crystal Shards</i>, Acro lives in a deep sea trench in Aqua Star.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bohboh">Bohboh</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=112" title="Edit section: Bohboh">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Bohboh</b> is a fiery <a href="/wiki/Owl" title="Owl">owl</a> with a <a href="/wiki/Raccoon" title="Raccoon">raccoon</a>-like tail that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Squeak_Squad" title="Kirby: Squeak Squad">Kirby: Squeak Squad</a></i>. Bohboh resides at Vocal Volcano. During the fight, Bohboh attacks by dropping fireballs and attempting to throw Kirby into the lava pool.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Chameleo_Arm">Chameleo Arm</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=113" title="Edit section: Chameleo Arm">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Chameleo Arm</b> first appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star</a></i> and its remake. It is a large <a href="/wiki/Chameleon" title="Chameleon">chameleon</a>-type creature who can change color. Its eyes are massive and it has two clawed and stretchable legs on the back of its lower spine. He is found as a boss in "Milky Way Wishes", "The Great Cave Offensive", "Helper To Hero", and "The Arena". It is also referred to as Ghameleo Arm.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Computer_Virus">Computer Virus</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=114" title="Edit section: Computer Virus">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b><a href="/wiki/Computer_virus" title="Computer virus">Computer Virus</a></b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">バトル・ウィンドウズ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Batoru Windōzu</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a boss in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star</a></i>. It appears as a boss of the sub-games "The Great Cave Offensive" and "Milky Way Wishes". It behaves like a malfunctioning <a href="/wiki/Role-playing_game" title="Role-playing game">role-playing game</a> with turn-based events where if the enemy turns, Kirby cannot harm them and the enemies do not attack in Kirby's turn. In "The Great Cave Offensive", Computer Virus uses Slime, <a href="/wiki/Puppet" title="Puppet">Puppet</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Magician_(fantasy)" title="Magician (fantasy)">Magician</a> to attack Kirby. For "Milky Way Wishes", Computer Virus uses Magician, Evil <a href="/wiki/Knight" title="Knight">Knight</a>, and Great <a href="/wiki/Dragon" title="Dragon">Dragon</a> to attack Kirby.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fatty_Whale">Fatty Whale</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=115" title="Edit section: Fatty Whale">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Fatty <a href="/wiki/Whale" title="Whale">Whale</a></b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ファッティ・ホエール</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Fatti Hoēru</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a boss in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star</a></i> and its remake. Fatty Whale is a sailor whale who smokes and attacks Kirby in water. He is battled in "The Great Cave Offense", "Milky Way Wishes", "Helper To Hero", and "The Arena". His attacks consist of blasting water from his pipe or blowhole to throw Kirby around and knock debris from the ceiling onto him, and also rolling and bellyflopping onto him.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Galacta_Knight">Galacta Knight</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=116" title="Edit section: Galacta Knight">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Galacta Knight</b> is the greatest warrior in the galaxy. His first appearance is in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star#Remake" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star Ultra</a></i>, as the final boss of "Meta Knightmare Ultra". He performs unusual attacks with his sword, consisting of swipes, tornadoes, and energy blasts. He appears when Meta Knight, done with his training, wishes to the reformed Nova to fight the strongest warrior in the galaxy. Nova grants this by allowing a challenge with Galacta Knight, whom is said by Nova to have been sealed away in ancient times for fear that his power was too great. He has a white mask with a plus sign on it and a hot pink body. His eyes are red and glow just like Meta Knight's, except Galacta Knight's eyes are more rectangular. He wields a purple lance with a white shield that has a purple cross on the front. As for his wings, they are angel-like and glow white. He must also be faced in The True Arena, in which he is one of the Final Four and is fought as the penultimate boss.</p>
<p>He also appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Return_to_Dream_Land" title="Kirby's Return to Dream Land">Kirby's Return to Dream Land</a></i>, fought right before Magolor EX in that game's own True Arena mode as a secret boss. In the Meta Knightmare sub-game of <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Planet_Robobot" title="Kirby: Planet Robobot">Kirby: Planet Robobot</a></i>, Star Dream summons Galacta Knight as Meta Knight's final opponent, but Galacta Knight destroys Star Dream before fighting Meta Knight again.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Grand_Doomer">Grand Doomer</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=117" title="Edit section: Grand Doomer">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <b>Grand Doomer</b> is the ruler or master of all Sphere Doomers. He appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Return_to_Dream_Land" title="Kirby's Return to Dream Land">Kirby's Return to Dream Land</a></i> as a main boss when beating planet Pop Star. He is much more advanced than the miniature Sphere Doomers because of its health and attack. The Grand Doomer is golden with dark red eyes and is very shiny. He is faced against Kirby in The Arena and the Nutty Noon. He has a bunch of attacks familiar to "Dyna Blade". His attacks are laying or spreading fireballs and hides in shadows or black holes then pop out at you. The Grand Doomer is also the Boss carries the last piece to Magolar's ship, which is the mast.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Heavy_Lobster">Heavy Lobster</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=118" title="Edit section: Heavy Lobster">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
