<p><b>Heavy Lobster</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ヘビーロブスター</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Hebī Robusutā</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a strong mechanical <a href="/wiki/Lobster" title="Lobster">lobster</a>-like monster that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star</a></i>. It attacks Kirby multiple times during his assault on the Halberd. In the <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> episode "Combat Kirby", Heavy Lobster is one of Nightmare's strongest creations. Nightmare sends Heavy Lobster to track down and rip apart the Halberd. It took the combined attacks of Ice Kirby, Sword Knight, and Blade Knight to destroy Heavy Lobster.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Heavy_Mole">Heavy Mole</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=119" title="Edit section: Heavy Mole">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Heavy Mole</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ヘビーモール</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Hebī Mōru</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a mechanical monster that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Adventure" title="Kirby's Adventure">Kirby's Adventure</a></i>. It is the boss of Yogurt Yard.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ice_Dragon">Ice Dragon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=120" title="Edit section: Ice Dragon">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <b>Ice <a href="/wiki/Dragon" title="Dragon">Dragon</a></b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">アイスドラゴン</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Aisu Doragon</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a <a href="/wiki/Dinosaur" title="Dinosaur">dinosaur</a>-like monster that appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_2" title="Kirby's Dream Land 2">Kirby's Dream Land 2</a></i>. It is the boss of the Iceberg. In <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_3" title="Kirby's Dream Land 3">Kirby's Dream Land 3</a></i>, Ice Dragon is drawn up by Ado. In Kirby: Planet Robobot, a solid hologram of Ice Dragon appears as one of the four bosses summoned by the Holo Defense API, and is known as Holo-Ice Dragon.</p>
<p>In the <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> episode "Dedede's Snow Job", King Dedede orders Ice Dragon from Nightmare Enterprise in order to combat the heat wave in Cappy Town. Kirby, Tiff, and Tuff later find the Ice Dragon in its mature state where it ends up attacking Chilly. Kirby becomes Ice Kirby and freezes the Ice Dragon from within. Once the Ice Dragon is destroyed, all the snow and Chilly begins to melt. In "Labor Daze", King Dedede uses the Cappies that he enlisted to work at his newly built factory to build a robot replica of the Ice Dragon. Ice Kirby freezes the factory's boiler enough to destroy the Ice Dragon Robot and the factory with the destroyed environment also being restored.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Kabula">Kabula</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=121" title="Edit section: Kabula">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Kabula</b> (spelled <b>Kaboola</b> in <i>Kirby's Dream Land</i> and appearing as <b>Core Kabula</b> in <i>Planet Robobot</i>) is King Dedede's blimp, who appears as a boss in some games. She has the ability to fire cannonballs and barrel-roll at Kirby, and Kirby must shoot her down by firing projectiles (air pellets in <i>Kirby's Dream Land</i>, the Starship in <i>Kirby Super Star Ultra</i>, and in the Robobot Armor's Jet Mode in <i>Kirby: Planet Robobot</i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Kracko">Kracko</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=122" title="Edit section: Kracko">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Kracko</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">クラッコ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Kurakko</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a boss that first appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land" title="Kirby's Dream Land">Kirby's Dream Land</a></i>. It resembles a large <a href="/wiki/Cumulus_cloud" title="Cumulus cloud">cumulus cloud</a> with spikes protruding from all sides, and a single large eyeball in the center. It attacks with electricity, rain, and by producing smaller enemies, such as Waddle Doos. Kracko is typically first seen in a weaker form, sometimes called Kracko Jr. Its characteristic eye remains, but it is surrounded by four balls, which it either spins slowly or launches at Kirby. This form either fights as a mini-boss earlier in various games, or immediately prior to transforming to its "adult" form. Kracko is slightly different in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star</a></i> (Ultra) in that Kracko Jr. and Kracko are two separate bosses. In <i>Kirby's Dream Land 3</i>, an illusion of Kracko in its adult form is drawn up and brought to life by Ado to fight for her, and is the last monster to be drawn. Kracko returns in the <i>Kirby Super Star Ultra</i> sub-game "Revenge of the King" sub-game as Kracko Jr.'s Revenge and Kracko's Revenge, each with purple <a href="/wiki/Sclera" title="Sclera">scleras</a> and dark grey cloud-parts.</p>
<p>Kracko appears in the <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> episode "Dark and Stormy Knight" where it appears as a monster purchased by King Dedede from Nightmare Enterprises to defeat Kirby. For most of the episode, Kracko appeared as a storm cloud that shot lightning throughout Cappytown. But when Kirby flew inside it, Kracko shot electric sword beams at Kirby, giving him the sword ability. Kirby shot five sword beams back with the last one splitting Kracko in half. Kracko was shown the same way he is in the games.</p>
<p>Kracko is also a surprise boss in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_%26_the_Amazing_Mirror" title="Kirby &amp; the Amazing Mirror">Kirby &amp; the Amazing Mirror</a></i>. Unlike most bosses in Kirby and the Amazing Mirror, Kracko is not a mirror copy, but has no copy and is the original boss. In <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Squeak_Squad" title="Kirby: Squeak Squad">Kirby: Squeak Squad</a></i>, a gray, robot version called Mecha Kracko appears as a boss.</p>
<p>In <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Triple_Deluxe" title="Kirby: Triple Deluxe">Kirby: Triple Deluxe</a></i>, Kracko returns as a boss, encountered in Old Odyssey. According to its in-game description, it has made Floralia part of its territory and is being fed by a mysterious power source, making its attacks stronger than ever before. In Dededetour, King Dedede fights <b>Kracko DX</b>, Kracko's stronger form.</p>
<p>In <i>Kirby: Planet Robobot</i>, a solid hologram of Kracko appears as one of the four bosses summoned by the Holo Defense API, and is known as Holo-Kracko.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Lololo_and_Lalala">Lololo and Lalala</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=123" title="Edit section: Lololo and Lalala">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Lololo and Lalala</b> appear once as the second boss fight in <i>Kirby's Dream Land</i>, where they push objects in an attempt to hurt Kirby. They appear to be parodies of Lolo and Lala, the protagonists of HAL's <i>Eggerland/Adventures of Lolo</i> series of games.</p>
<p>They also appear in <i>Kirby Super Star</i> sub-game "Spring Breeze" as bosses, and in the <i>Kirby Super Star Ultra</i> sub-game "Revenge of the King", they return as <b>Lololo and Lalala's Revenge</b>.</p>
<p>They appear in the anime as friendly characters, where they are known as <b>Fololo and Falala</b> in the English dub, and they reside in King Dedede's castle. They are originally a single monster created by Nightmare Enterprises called <b>Lola</b> (ロラ <i>Rora</i>, <b>Fofa</b> in the English dub), but it is split into two by Slice n' Splice and sent to Dedede at the suggestion to the Nightmare Enterprise Salesman by Nightmare. In the Japanese version of the anime, Lololo is voiced by Chiro Kanzaki and Lalala is voiced by Madoki Akita. In the English dub, they are both voiced by <a href="/wiki/Veronica_Taylor" title="Veronica Taylor">Veronica Taylor</a>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Meta-Knights">Meta-Knights</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=124" title="Edit section: Meta-Knights">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <b>Meta-Knights</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">メタナイツ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Meta-Naitsu</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> are a group of soldiers led by <a href="/wiki/List_of_Kirby_characters#Meta_Knight" title="List of Kirby characters">Meta Knight</a>, who often uses them to test Kirby's skills throughout <a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Adventure" title="Kirby's Adventure">Kirby's Adventure</a>, which is their first appearance. The Meta-Knights include <b>Axe Knight</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">アックスナイト</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Akkusu Naito</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span>, <b>Mace Knight</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">メイスナイト</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Meisu Naito</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span>, <b>Javelin Knight</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ジャベリンナイト</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Jaberin Naito</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span>, and <b>Trident Knight</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">トライデントナイト</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Toraidento Naito</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span>. They are four distinct armored soldiers that each wield the weapon they are named after. The Meta-Knights return prominently in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star</a></i>, where they aided Meta Knight in his attempt to conquer Dream Land via his armored airship, the Halberd. They also appeared in some other game modes, also fighting as a team. A version of them can also be summoned by Galacta Knight.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mr._Shine_and_Mr._Bright">Mr. Shine and Mr. Bright</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=125" title="Edit section: Mr. Shine and Mr. Bright">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Mr. Shine &amp; Mr. Bright</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ミスターシャイン&amp;ミスターブライト</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Misutā Shain &amp; Misutā Buraito</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> are tag-team bosses first appearing in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Adventure" title="Kirby's Adventure">Kirby's Adventure</a></i>. Mr. Shine appears as a crescent <a href="/wiki/Moon" title="Moon">moon</a> with a face and limbs, while Mr. Bright is a <a href="/wiki/Sun" title="Sun">sun</a> with similar features. They are the Sun and the Moon in Dreamland. One always stays in the air, raining down projectiles, while the other attacks from the ground. One of their most lethal attacks is when they create a solar eclipse: Mr. Bright will blast the area with flames while Mr. Shine creates a patch of shadow, which is the only safe spot. They return in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_2" title="Kirby's Dream Land 2">Kirby's Dream Land 2</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Dream_Land_3" title="Kirby's Dream Land 3">Kirby's Dream Land 3</a></i>, and <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Adventure#Remakes_and_ports" title="Kirby's Adventure">Kirby: Nightmare in Dreamland</a></i>. In <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star</a></i>, they literally fought day and night due to a misunderstanding caused by Marx. In the anime, a monster named Slice and Splice in the English dub and Kittari Hattari in the Japanese version uses moon- and sun-shaped staffs to split and paste his enemies. Presumably, this was a nod to Mr. Shine and Mr. Bright. They also appear in <i>Kirby Mass Attack</i> on Strato Patrol EOS mode.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Paintra">Paintra</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=126" title="Edit section: Paintra">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Paintra</b> is a mysterious paint <a href="/wiki/Witchcraft" title="Witchcraft">witch</a> who appears as a boss in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Triple_Deluxe" title="Kirby: Triple Deluxe">Kirby: Triple Deluxe</a></i>. She has paintbrushes for legs (which she can combine into one paintbrush) and uses many paint based attacks. Some examples of her attacks include one where she paints over the screen, making seeing her more difficult, and one where she rains down paint across the arena. Her pause screen description speaks of a painting that depicted two sisters who were separated at birth. This painting hung unnoticed in a painter's studio for many years but later became sentient and vowed revenge. She is encountered in Lollipop Land. She also has a more vicious form known as <b>Paintra DX</b>, which is battled in Dededetour and the True Arena.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Paint_Roller">Paint Roller</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=127" title="Edit section: Paint Roller">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Paint Roller</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ペイントローラー</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Peinto Rōrā</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> appears as a boss in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Adventure" title="Kirby's Adventure">Kirby's Adventure</a></i>, <i>Kirby: Nightmare in Dreamland</i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Canvas_Curse" title="Kirby: Canvas Curse">Kirby: Canvas Curse</a></i>. It wears a baseball cap and roller skates, and it is capable of drawing enemies that come to life. It appears in the anime as a monster bought by Dedede to fight Kirby.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Poppy_Bros._Jr._and_Poppy_Bros._Sr.">Poppy Bros. Jr. and Poppy Bros. Sr.</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=128" title="Edit section: Poppy Bros. Jr. and Poppy Bros. Sr.">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Poppy Bros. Jr</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ポピーブロス·ジュニア</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Popī Burozu Junia</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span>. is an <a href="/wiki/Elf" title="Elf">elf</a>-like enemy seen in many games. They may either be unarmed, throw bombs, or throw boomerangs, and are sometimes found balancing on apples, Maxim Tomatoes, or riding on a mount. He is the Helper assigned to the Bomb ability in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star#Remake" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star Ultra</a></i>. <b>Poppy Bros. Sr.</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ポピーブラザーズ·シニア</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Popī Burazāzu Shinia</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> serves as a boss and is a larger version of the Bomb version of Poppy Bros. Jr. They sometimes give Kirby the Bomb or Cutter ability, though most often the former. Poppy Bros. Jr. also makes a cameo appearance in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Right_Back_at_Ya!" title="Kirby: Right Back at Ya!">Kirby: Right Back at Ya!</a></i> as a monster in training.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pyribbit">Pyribbit</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=129" title="Edit section: Pyribbit">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Pyribbit</b> is a giant <a href="/wiki/Frog" title="Frog">frog</a> enemy who appears as a boss in <a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Triple_Deluxe" title="Kirby: Triple Deluxe">Kirby: Triple Deluxe</a>. He is at home in a volcanic environment: his pause screen description states that he uses lava for bath water and likes to hop around. He mainly uses fire and lava based attacks in battle such as fire breath or lava pillars that race towards the platform Kirby stands on. He is found in Endless Explosions and has a more powerful form called <b>Pyribbit DX</b>, fought in Dededetour and the True Arena.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sphere_Doomer_2">Sphere Doomer</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=130" title="Edit section: Sphere Doomer">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <b>Sphere Doomer</b> is a mini mysterious boss in "<a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Return_to_Dream_Land" title="Kirby's Return to Dream Land">Kirby's Return to Dream Land</a>". He is a miniature and easier version of the Grand Doomer. They are very similar to Dyna Blade attacks. They are shaped like spheres with wings and they can be in different colors. When you beat them, you earn two energy spheres. You can find them in different dimensions.</p>
<p>In Kirby: Planet Robobot, solid holograms of two Sphere Doomers appear as one of the four bosses summoned by the Holo Defense API, and are known as Holo-Sphere Doomers.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Squeaks">The Squeaks</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=131" title="Edit section: The Squeaks">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <b>Squeaks</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ドロッチェ団</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Dorotche Dan</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> are an <a href="/wiki/Infamy" title="Infamy">infamous</a> band of robbers who are the villains in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Squeak_Squad" title="Kirby: Squeak Squad">Kirby: Squeak Squad</a></i>. When Kirby's cake disappears, Kirby thinks King Dedede took it, but he then finds out the Squeaks stole his cake. Kirby follows the Squeaks throughout the game trying to get his cake back. The Squeaks also stole a treasure chest which Kirby thinks has his cake inside. Kirby has to fight Daroach, leader of the Squeaks, at the end of World 6. Once Daroach is beaten, Meta Knight comes out of nowhere and takes the chest. Kirby follows Meta Knight throughout World 7. At World 7's end Kirby fights Meta Knight for the chest. Once Kirby beats Meta Knight, he takes the chest, but the Squeaks come and take it from him. Daroach opens the chest, but instead of the cake, he finds a dark cloud that grabs him. Kirby chases after the cloud in World 8, and eventually fights Dark Daroach. Once Kirby beats it, the dark cloud lets out Daroach. It floats away as a small, black star. Kirby follows the star until it becomes its true form, a dark star called Dark Nebula. Using the Triple Star Rod Daroach gave him, Kirby defeats Dark Nebula. Once Dark Nebula is beaten, you beat <i>Kirby: Squeak Squad</i>. The ending shows Kirby flying back home wondering where his cake went. The Squeaks give Kirby his cake back as an apology for the trouble they put Kirby into. It turns out Meta Knight didn't give Kirby the chest because he didn't want Kirby to let out Dark Nebula.</p>
<p>The Squeaks later appear in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Mass_Attack" title="Kirby Mass Attack">Kirby Mass Attack</a></i>, where they give Kirby hints on where medals are. For some reason, Daroach doesn't seem to remember Kirby after their last encounter.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wham_Bam_Rock">Wham Bam Rock</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=132" title="Edit section: Wham Bam Rock">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Wham Bam Rock</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ワムバムロック</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Wamu Bamu Rokku</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> first appeared in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star</a></i>, and resembled a tribal head with two floating stone hands. Its motives are unknown, and it appeared as both the final boss of The Great Cave Offensive and as a normal boss character in "Milky Way Wishes". In <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star#Remake" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star Ultra</a></i>, it was redesigned to look less organic, though some aspects of its previous design were incorporated into a stronger variant named <b>Wham Bam Jewel</b>. Wearing a jeweled crown with swinging <a href="/wiki/Diamond" title="Diamond">diamond</a> earrings, fangs, and three eyes, it serves as the final boss in the <a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star#Remake" title="Kirby Super Star">Helper to Hero</a> boss rush along with Wham Bam Rock. Kirby must also defeat his standalone self as the second of the final four bosses in "The True Arena". One of his attacks is a reference to the <a href="/wiki/Finger_gun" title="Finger gun">finger gun</a>, in which he points at Kirby and fires. Wham Bam Rock is possibly the inspiration for Master Hand in the <i><a href="/wiki/Super_Smash_Bros." title="Super Smash Bros.">Super Smash Bros.</a></i> series.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Whispy_Woods">Whispy Woods</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=133" title="Edit section: Whispy Woods">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Whispy Woods</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ウィスピーウッズ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Wisupī Uzzu</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a large apple tree whose most common attack is dropping apples from his branches. He generally appears as a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Boss_(video_games)" title="Boss (video games)">boss</a>, usually the first one in many Kirby games and the first boss to appear in the Kirby series. Also, in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star" title="Kirby Super Star">Kirby Super Star</a></i> (and <a href="/wiki/Kirby_Super_Star#Remake" title="Kirby Super Star">its remake</a>) there exists a related pair of creatures named Twin Woods, and they can be found in Milky Way Wishes, Revenge of Meta Knight, Meta Knightmare Ultra, The Arena, and Helper to Hero. In "Revenge of the King", Whispy Woods comes back as <b>Whispy's Revenge</b>. This time, its leaves are purple and it can drop poisonous apples and worms. It can also drop Gordos like Twin Woods, and shoot gusts of wind and small twisters.</p>
<p>Whispy makes appearances in the <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Super_Smash_Bros._(series)" title="Super Smash Bros. (series)">Super Smash Bros. series</a></i>. He can be seen in Kirby-based stages, blowing wind at the characters and dropping apples.</p>
<p>In <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kirby_and_the_Amazing_Mirror" title="Kirby and the Amazing Mirror">Kirby and the Amazing Mirror</a></i>, a similar creature called King Golem appears, its appearance and attacks identical to that of Whispy Woods. In <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby:_Triple_Deluxe" title="Kirby: Triple Deluxe">Kirby: Triple Deluxe</a></i>, Whispy appears as a stage in <i>Kirby Fighters</i> multiplayer. In Story Mode, Taranza uses his power on a nearby plant which grows into <b>Flowery Woods</b> and is the games first boss. Unlike Whispy Woods, Flowery Woods can uproot itself and can attack using its roots. In <i>Dededetour</i>, King Dedede's first boss is <b>Flowery Woods DX</b>. According to it in-game description, Flowery Woods &amp; Flowery Woods DX relation to Whispy Woods is unclear. In Kirby: Planet Robobot, a mechanical version of Whispy appears called <b>Clanky Woods</b>..</p>
<p>The anime features him as the king of the forest in Dream Land. Whispy is several hundred years old, and very wise, though he has a bit of a temper. He's very kind to his friends, but shows no mercy to those that threaten his kingdom. At first, he believes Kirby and his friends are intruders when they build a campfire around him. It turns out to be a setup by Dedede, who wants to destroy Whispy to build a golf course. After most of the forest is cut down, it is revived by one of Whispy's apples. Dedede continues to constantly try to build his golf course during the series while Whispy becomes Kirby's ally. It is voiced by <a href="/wiki/Osamu_Hosoi" title="Osamu Hosoi">Osamu Hosoi</a> in the Japanese version of the anime and by <a href="/wiki/Dan_Green_(voice_actor)" title="Dan Green (voice actor)">Dan Green</a> in the English dub.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Kirby.27s_Epic_Yarn_Bosses"><i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Epic_Yarn" title="Kirby's Epic Yarn">Kirby's Epic Yarn</a></i> Bosses</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=134" title="Edit section: Kirby's Epic Yarn Bosses">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The first four bosses of this game are creations of the sorcerer Yin-Yarn, each being a guardian of one piece of magic yarn; they have not been seen in any other Kirby game.</p>
<ul>
<li>The boss of Grass Land is <b>Fangora</b>, a <a href="/wiki/Dragon" title="Dragon">dragon</a> who attacks with its long tongue, strong winds creates with its wings, and fireballs.</li>
<li>The boss of Hot Land is <b>Hot Wings</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">フェニクロウ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Fenikurou</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span>, a flaming <a href="/wiki/Phoenix_(mythology)" title="Phoenix (mythology)">phoenix</a> named after the chicken dish, who attacks by shooting fireballs, charging at the player, and summoning enemies.</li>
<li>The boss of Treat Land is <b>Squashini</b> (his name is a portmanteau of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Squash_(plant)" title="Squash (plant)">squash</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Houdini" title="Houdini">Houdini</a>), a <a href="/wiki/Pumpkin" title="Pumpkin">pumpkin</a>-headed <a href="/wiki/Magician_(fantasy)" title="Magician (fantasy)">magician</a> who attacks you with varying magic tricks, selected by a randomised <a href="/wiki/Slot_machine" title="Slot machine">slot machine</a>.</li>
<li>Water Land's boss is <b>Capamari</b> (a play on "calamari", also known as Stylocto on the American website), a gigantic <a href="/wiki/Squid" title="Squid">squid</a> with a nightcap on its head.</li>
</ul>
<p>Later bosses in the game are more familiar.</p>
<ul>
<li>Snow Land's boss is yarn version of King Dedede, who was teleported to Patch Land by Yin-Yarn, and transformed into a marionette (Kirby can free him by pulling at all the buttons holding him up).</li>
<li>The boss of Space Land is Meta Knight, also teleported by Yin-Yarn and brainwashed using a set of enchanted swords (after defeating him, Meta-Knight and Kirby team up).</li>
<li>Whispy Woods, Kracko, and the Main Cannon and Reactor of <i>Halberd</i> appear as mini-bosses in Dream Land, and the final boss is Yin-Yarn himself, who assumes two different forms, Yin-Yarn and Mega Yin-Yarn.</li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Anime_characters">Anime characters</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=135" title="Edit section: Anime characters">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Escargoon">Escargoon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=136" title="Edit section: Escargoon">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Escargoon</b> (<b>Doctor Escargon</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ドクター・エスカルゴン</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Dokutā Esukarugon</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> in Japanese versions) is a purple <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Anthropomorphic" title="Anthropomorphic">anthropomorphic</a> <a href="/wiki/Snail" title="Snail">snail</a> that serves King Dedede in the anime series. He originally left his mother's farm to become famous and make his mother proud, but ended up serving Dedede instead as his <a href="/wiki/Personal_assistant" title="Personal assistant">personal assistant</a>. He helps Dedede's plots by creating various inventions to help defeat Kirby. King Dedede smashes Escargoon as much as he does Kirby, but his loyalty never waivers. Escargoon has a <a href="/wiki/Goatee" title="Goatee">goatee</a>. He is voiced by <a href="/wiki/Naoki_Tatsuta" title="Naoki Tatsuta">Naoki Tatsuta</a> in the Japanese version and by <a href="/wiki/Ted_Lewis_(voice_actor)" title="Ted Lewis (voice actor)">Ted Lewis</a> in the English dub.</p>
<p>Although he was an anime-exclusive character, Escargoon makes a cameo appearance in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Mass_Attack" title="Kirby Mass Attack">Kirby Mass Attack</a></i>, as part of one of King Dedede's attacks (along with several Waddle Dees) in the subgame <i>Kirby Quest</i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sir_Ebrum_.26_Lady_Like">Sir Ebrum &amp; Lady Like</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=137" title="Edit section: Sir Ebrum &amp; Lady Like">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Sir Ebrum</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">パーム</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Pāmu</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> and <b>Lady Like</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">メーム</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Mēmu</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> are the parents of Tiff and Tuff, who work and live in King Dedede's Castle and keep peace between their strong-willed offsprings and their rambunctious employer. Sir Ebrum works as the <a href="/wiki/Minister_(government)" title="Minister (government)">Cabinet Minister</a>. Lady Like is usually the one out of the two who is suspicious of Dedede's plots since they put her children in danger as well, although even Sir Ebrum gets suspicious sometimes.</p>
<p>Sir Ebrum is voiced by <a href="/wiki/Takashi_Nagasako" title="Takashi Nagasako">Takashi Nagasako</a> in the Japanese version and David Lapkin in the English dub. Lady Like is voiced by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Yuko_Mizutani" title="Yuko Mizutani">Yuko Mizutani</a> in the Japanese version and <a href="/wiki/Kayzie_Rogers" title="Kayzie Rogers">Kayzie Rogers</a> impersonating <a href="/wiki/Eva_Gabor" title="Eva Gabor">Eva Gabor</a> in the English dub.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tiff_and_Tuff">Tiff and Tuff</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=138" title="Edit section: Tiff and Tuff">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Tiff</b> and <b>Tuff</b> (Fūmu <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">フーム</span><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> and Bun <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ブン</span><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> in the Japanese versions) are the brother and sister duo that accompany Kirby in the anime series where they are the children of Sir Ebrum and Lady Like. They live in the castle of King Dedede with their parents and help Kirby in his fight against Dedede's plots and Nightmare's monsters. Tiff is more interested in academics such as chemistry and other studies while Tuff is active in sports and other physical activities.</p>
<p>Tiff is voiced by <a href="/wiki/Sayuri_Yoshida" title="Sayuri Yoshida">Sayuri Yoshida</a> in the original Japanese version and <a href="/wiki/Kerry_Williams" title="Kerry Williams">Kerry Williams</a> in the English dub. Tuff is voiced by <a href="/wiki/Rika_Komatsu" title="Rika Komatsu">Rika Komatsu</a> in the Japanese version and <a href="/wiki/Kayzie_Rogers" title="Kayzie Rogers">Kayzie Rogers</a> in the English dub.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Biblio">Biblio</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=139" title="Edit section: Biblio">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Biblio</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ビブリ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Biburi</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a Cappy who wears glasses and runs a <a href="/wiki/Bookselling" title="Bookselling">book store</a> in Cappy Town. He first appeared in "Watermelon Felon" and serves as one of the later introduced characters in the anime.</p>
<p>He is voiced by <a href="/wiki/Maddie_Blaustein" title="Maddie Blaustein">Maddie Blaustein</a> in the English dub.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Chief_Bookem">Chief Bookem</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=140" title="Edit section: Chief Bookem">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Chief Bookem</b> is a Cappy <a href="/wiki/Chief_of_police" title="Chief of police">police chief</a> who is the only <a href="/wiki/Police_officer" title="Police officer">police officer</a> in Cappy Town. He has a large grey <a href="/wiki/Moustache" title="Moustache">mustache</a> and lives in his house/police station with his wife Buttercup. There isn't much for him to do, but doesn't let that discourage him. One day, Bookem notices a notorious Cappy criminal Doron causing trouble in Cappy Town, he puts Doron in jail. In the episode "Hail to the Chief", he said that he was a former member of a military group called the Rough Ranger Corps. This, however, turned out to be a false story he told to the children of Cappy Town to entertain them and it was his brother who was in the Rangers.</p>
<p>He is voiced by <a href="/wiki/Atsushi_Kisaichi" title="Atsushi Kisaichi">Atsushi Kisaichi</a> in the Japanese version. In the English dub, Chief Bookum is voiced by <a href="/wiki/Jerry_Lobozzo" title="Jerry Lobozzo">Jerry Lobozzo</a> from episode 1 to 75 and by <a href="/wiki/Andrew_Rannells" title="Andrew Rannells">Andrew Rannells</a> from episode 75 to 100.</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Buttercup">Buttercup</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=141" title="Edit section: Buttercup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><b>Buttercup</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">サト</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Sato</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is the loving wife of Chief Bookem.</p>
<p>She is voiced by Madoka Akita in the Japanese version and by <a href="/wiki/Lisa_Ortiz" title="Lisa Ortiz">Lisa Ortiz</a> in the English dub.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Doron">Doron</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=142" title="Edit section: Doron">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Doron</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ドロン</span><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a Cappy <a href="/wiki/Crime" title="Crime">criminal</a> who often commits crimes in Cappy Town such as <a href="/wiki/Shoplifting" title="Shoplifting">shoplifting</a> and stealing stuff from the citizens and is often seen in a jail cell at the Cappy Town Police Station. He has a circle-shaped <a href="/wiki/Beard" title="Beard">beard</a>. Based on the tendency to steal items, Doron is likely to be a <a href="/wiki/Kleptomania" title="Kleptomania">kleptomaniac</a>; this is supported by the fact that he stole a <a href="/wiki/Portrait" title="Portrait">portrait</a> from King Dedede's <a href="/wiki/Art_museum" title="Art museum">art gallery</a> in "Dedede's Monsterpiece" and runs away with Sir Ebrum's <a href="/wiki/Ring_(jewellery)" title="Ring (jewellery)">ring</a> in "The Thing About the Ring".</p>
<p>He is voiced by <a href="/wiki/Nobuo_Tobita" title="Nobuo Tobita">Nobuo Tobita</a> in the Japanese version.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gengu">Gengu</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=143" title="Edit section: Gengu">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Gengu</b> is a Cappy who is the <a href="/wiki/Shopkeeper" title="Shopkeeper">shopkeeper</a> of a <a href="/wiki/Toy_store" title="Toy store">toy store</a> in Cappy Town and also a good toy designer. Gengu would sometimes be seen with Tuggle. He carries a <a href="/wiki/Wrench" title="Wrench">wrench</a> at times.</p>
<p>He is voiced by Mizuki Saitoh in the Japanese version and by <a href="/wiki/Maddie_Blaustein" title="Maddie Blaustein">Maddie Blaustein</a> in the English dub.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gus">Gus</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=144" title="Edit section: Gus">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Gus</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ガス</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Gasu</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is an <a href="/wiki/Overall" title="Overall">overall</a>-wearing Cappy who is a skilled <a href="/wiki/Mechanic" title="Mechanic">mechanic</a> and the owner of a <a href="/wiki/Filling_station" title="Filling station">gas station</a>. He employed Kirby for a short period, but since only King Dedede and the Mayor have cars, it doesn't seem like he'd get much of his business, but he also fixes King Dedede's car every time it's damaged.</p>
<p>He is voiced by Osamu Hasoi in the Japanese version and by <a href="/wiki/Eric_Stuart" title="Eric Stuart">Eric Stuart</a> in the English dub.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Honey">Honey</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=145" title="Edit section: Honey">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Honey</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ハニー</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Hanī</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a Cappy Kid who is one of Tuff's friends. She is shown to be clingy to Spikehead at specific moments. Honey is also Spikehead's girlfriend.</p>
<p>She is voiced by Madoka Akita in the Japanese version and by <a href="/wiki/Kayzie_Rogers" title="Kayzie Rogers">Kayzie Rogers</a> in the English dub.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Iro">Iro</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=146" title="Edit section: Iro">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Iro</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ホッヘ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Hohhe</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a Cappy Kid who is wearing a <a href="/wiki/Beige" title="Beige">beige</a> <a href="/wiki/Top_hat" title="Top hat">flat top hat</a> and a green <a href="/wiki/Shirt" title="Shirt">shirt</a> and one of Tuff's friends. He is known for pulling pranks and causing trouble for the Cappies.</p>
<p>Iro is voiced by <a href="/wiki/Makiko_Ohmoto" title="Makiko Ohmoto">Makiko Ohmoto</a> in the Japanese version and by Kevin Kolack in the English dub.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mabel">Mabel</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=147" title="Edit section: Mabel">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Mabel</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">メーベル</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Mēberu</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a Cappy who is Cappy Town's residential <a href="/wiki/Fortune-telling" title="Fortune-telling">fortune teller</a>. The Cappies often go to her in order to have their future predicted or to help solve their woes. Later in the series, Mabel reveals that she really doesn't have any psychic powers, but still takes delight in helping the Cappies solve their problems. Mabel simply listens to what Samo overhears at the bar. After learning what is on each of the Cappies' minds, she can easily give them advice in the form of one of her predictions.</p>
<p>Mabel is voiced by <a href="/wiki/Y%C5%ABko_Mizutani" title="Yūko Mizutani">Yūko Mizutani</a> in the Japanese version and by <a href="/wiki/Lisa_Ortiz" title="Lisa Ortiz">Lisa Ortiz</a> in the English dub.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mayor_Len_Blustergas">Mayor Len Blustergas</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=148" title="Edit section: Mayor Len Blustergas">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b><a href="/wiki/Mayor" title="Mayor">Mayor</a> Len Blustergas</b> is a Cappy who is the Mayor of Cappy Town. He lives with his wife Hana, his three grandchildren, and his large flock of sheep. Despite being the Mayor of Cappy Town however, he has little freedom to run it freely due to the dictatorship of King Dedede who sometimes enforces unfair laws for his own selfish deeds. Nonetheless, the town's Cappies continue to respect Mayor Len for his own efforts.</p>
<p>He is voiced by <a href="/wiki/Takashi_Nagasako" title="Takashi Nagasako">Takashi Nagasako</a> in the Japanese version and by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mike_Pollock" title="Mike Pollock">Mike Pollock</a> in the English dub.</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hana">Hana</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=149" title="Edit section: Hana">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><b>Hana</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ハナ</span><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a Cappy resident of Cappy Town and the wife of Mayor Len Blustergas.</p>
<p>She is voiced by <a href="/wiki/Kayzie_Rogers" title="Kayzie Rogers">Kayzie Rogers</a> in the English dub.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Melman">Melman</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=150" title="Edit section: Melman">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Melman</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">モソ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Moso</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is an elderly Cappy who is Cappy Town's residential <a href="/wiki/Mail_carrier" title="Mail carrier">mailman</a>. In the episode "Born to Be Mild" Pt. 2, it is discovered that Melman is also the legendary <a href="/wiki/Outlaw_motorcycle_club" title="Outlaw motorcycle club">biker</a> Steppenwolf.</p>
<p>He is voiced by <a href="/wiki/Nobuo_Tobita" title="Nobuo Tobita">Nobuo Tobita</a> in the Japanese version and by <a href="/wiki/Maddie_Blaustein" title="Maddie Blaustein">Maddie Blaustein</a> in the English dub.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Professor_Curio">Professor Curio</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=151" title="Edit section: Professor Curio">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Professor Curio</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">キュリオ氏</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Kyurio Shi</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is an elderly Cappy who is a respected citizen of Cappy Town and carries his <a href="/wiki/Satchel" title="Satchel">satchel</a> at all times. Curio runs an <a href="/wiki/Antique_shop" title="Antique shop">antique shop</a>/<a href="/wiki/Museum" title="Museum">museum</a> where he displays his <a href="/wiki/Artifact_(archaeology)" title="Artifact (archaeology)">artifacts</a> of ancient Dream Land and a long lost Cappy civilization. Besides collecting ancient artifacts, Curio also finds <a href="/wiki/Consolation" title="Consolation">solace</a> by learning about the past in his free time as well.</p>
<p>He is voiced by Takeshi Nagasako in the Japanese version and by <a href="/wiki/Maddie_Blaustein" title="Maddie Blaustein">Maddie Blaustein</a> in the English dub.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Samo">Samo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=152" title="Edit section: Samo">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Samo</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">サモ</span><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a Cappy who is the owner and <a href="/wiki/Bartender" title="Bartender">bartender</a> of a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Juice_bar" title="Juice bar">juice bar</a> in Cappy Town. Upon hearing the problems of the Cappies that visit his bar, Samo would relay them to Mabel. He was one of the few who knew she wasn't a true psychic, not that he minded. They both care about each other, though Samo tends to get a bit sappy.</p>
<p>He is voiced by <a href="/wiki/Nobuo_Tobita" title="Nobuo Tobita">Nobuo Tobita</a> in the Japanese version and by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mike_Pollock" title="Mike Pollock">Mike Pollock</a> in the English dub.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sirica">Sirica</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=153" title="Edit section: Sirica">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Sirica</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">シリカ</span><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a pale and white alien girl who is the daughter of the legendary Star Warrior Garlude, a mother who teamed up with Meta Knight to reclaim Galaxia and was killed by a monster called Kirisakin. Sirica wields a weapon that can change into five different modes (a <a href="/wiki/Flamethrower" title="Flamethrower">flamethrower</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Grappling_hook" title="Grappling hook">grappling hook</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bazooka" title="Bazooka">bazooka</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Machine_gun" title="Machine gun">machine gun</a> and a <a href="/wiki/Sword" title="Sword">sword</a>). In the episode "Crusade for the Blade", she attacked Meta Knight and tried to seize his sword. She believed that he stole it and left her mother to be killed by the hands of Kirisakin, but was eventually proven wrong when she learned the truth from the sword. In the end, she helped Kirby to destroy Kirisakin, to avenge her mother's death and therefore becoming friends with him and the others. She later returned in the final episode, she is among the other characters as they help Kirby and his friends battle Nightmare.</p>
<p>She is voiced by <a href="/wiki/Tomoe_Hanba" title="Tomoe Hanba">Tomoe Hanba</a> in the Japanese version and by <a href="/wiki/Veronica_Taylor" title="Veronica Taylor">Veronica Taylor</a> in the English dub.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Spikehead">Spikehead</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=154" title="Edit section: Spikehead">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Spikehead</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">イロー</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Irō</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a Cappy Kid who is one of Tuff's friends and the pushiest amongst the three. Spikehead has a crush on Honey.</p>
<p>He is voiced by Chiro Kanzaki in the Japanese version and by <a href="/wiki/Amy_Birnbaum" title="Amy Birnbaum">Amy Birnbaum</a> in the English dub.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tuggle">Tuggle</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=155" title="Edit section: Tuggle">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Tuggle</b> is a Cappy who is the <a href="/wiki/Shopkeeper" title="Shopkeeper">shopkeeper</a> of Cappy Town's <a href="/wiki/Grocery_store" title="Grocery store">grocery store</a> which is one of a few places to get a steady flow of business. Tuggle would sometimes be see seen with Gengu. He wears a green hat and <a href="/wiki/Apron" title="Apron">apron</a> with two sun symbols in the bottom.</p>
<p>He is voiced by Mizuki Saitoh in the Japanese version and by <a href="/wiki/Eric_Stuart" title="Eric Stuart">Eric Stuart</a> in the English dub.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Yabui">Yabui</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=156" title="Edit section: Yabui">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Yabui</b> is a Cappy who is the only <a href="/wiki/Physician" title="Physician">doctor</a> in Cappy Town where he is also a <a href="/wiki/Dentist" title="Dentist">dentist</a>. He runs a small, low tech clinic, but doesn't get many bad cases aside from colds, toothaches, and the occasional case of sleeping sickness. Many of the Cappies don't like visiting Yabui as he has many painful strategies of fighting cavities. His eyes and mouth were hidden by his glasses and a light grey mustache respectively.</p>
<p>He is voiced by Sekine Kazunori in the Japanese version and by David Lapkin in the English dub.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Nightmare_Enterprises">Nightmare Enterprises</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=157" title="Edit section: Nightmare Enterprises">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>Nightmare Enterprises</b> (<i>Holy Nightmare Co.</i> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">ホーリーナイトメア社</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Hōrī Naitomea-sha</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> in the Japanese version and also known as N.M.E) is an organization led by Nightmare. Its purpose is creating monsters selling them to unsuspecting customers through the internet in order to spread Nightmare's empire. Besides the monsters and by-products, Nightmare Enterprises also creates different kinds of warfare, ranging from laser guns to large ships. The company is housed by a massive spaceship with an eye on its front and cyberspace cities on its exterior.</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Nightmare_Enterprises_Salesman">Nightmare Enterprises Salesman</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=158" title="Edit section: Nightmare Enterprises Salesman">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>One of Nightmare Enterprises' main employees is its <b>Salesman</b> (<i>Customer Service</i> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">カスタマーサービス</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Kasutamā Sābisu</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> in Japan), who sells monsters to King Dedede over the Internet. In the Japanese version, he speaks politely, but still doesn't pass up a chance to insult customers. However, in the dub, his personality is more like that of a stereotypical used car salesman. The Nightmare Enterprises Salesman answers to Nightmare and often tends to overcharge King Dedede for his purchases. In "New Year! Kirby Quiz Show" ("The Kirby Quiz" in the dub), he decided to host a quiz show to welcome the new year with questions about the series. Until the final episode, only the top half of his body is shown giving King Dedede and Escargoon the illusion of him being a tall human. In the finale, he is revealed to be very short where he has Kirby-like legs.</p>
<p>Although he is considered an anime only character, the Nightmare Enterprises Salesman appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Kirby_Mass_Attack" title="Kirby Mass Attack">Kirby Mass Attack</a></i> in the sub-game Strato Patrol EOS at the game over screen.</p>
<p>Salesman is voiced by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Banjo_Ginga" title="Banjo Ginga">Banjo Ginga</a> in the original version and by <a href="/wiki/Dan_Green_(voice_actor)" title="Dan Green (voice actor)">Dan Green</a> in the English Dub.</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Monsters">Monsters</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=159" title="Edit section: Monsters">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<table class="plainlinks metadata ambox mbox-small-left ambox-content" role="presentation">
<tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg"><img alt="[icon]" data-file-height="31" data-file-width="44" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/20px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/30px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/40px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 2x" width="20"/></a></td>
<td class="mbox-text"><span class="mbox-text-span"><b>This section needs expansion</b>. <small>You can help by <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=List_of_Kirby_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=">adding to it</a>.</small> <small><i>(November 2012)</i></small></span></td>
</tr>
</table>
<p><b>Monsters</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">魔獣</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Majū</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> are the fiendish creatures in the anime. They are created by Nightmare at Nightmare Enterprises where he has them sold for profit. Besides the monsters that appear in the video game, the following monsters are exclusive to the anime:</p>
<ul>
<li><b>Regular Monsters</b> - Regular Monsters are the common combatant monsters used by Nightmare Enterprises. There are different types of Regular Monsters in the series.
<ul>
<li><b>Mini-Monsters</b> - Mini-Monsters are small Monsters that cause trouble wherever they go. They come in the shape of <a href="/wiki/Axe" title="Axe">axes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Broom" title="Broom">brooms</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cattle" title="Cattle">cows</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cyclops" title="Cyclops">cyclopes</a>, four-armed <a href="/wiki/Boxing" title="Boxing">boxers</a>, <a href="/wiki/Raccoon" title="Raccoon">raccoons</a>, <a href="/wiki/Radish" title="Radish">radishes</a>, witch-hatted monsters, wood pieces, and <a href="/wiki/Wrench" title="Wrench">wrench</a>-armed robots. They had a small appearance in the beginning of "A Blockbuster Battle". The Mini-Monsters had a major part in "Monster Management" where Knuckle Joe worked for Nightmare Enterprises and sent the Mini-Monsters to Cappy Town to tire Kirby out enough for the Nightmare Enterprises Salesman to send Masher.</li>
<li><b>Chess Monsters</b> - Chess Monsters appeared in a flashback in "Kirby's Duel Role" where Kabu mentioned that there was one monster that Nightmare created that didn't follow his orders. In "Fight to the Finish", the Chess Monsters were seen in Nightmare's lair where they are shown to be larger and much different in appearances.</li>
<li><b>Generic Monsters</b> - Generic Monsters are Nightmare Enterprises' most important Monsters. There are 13 different generic monsters ranging from green gem-wearing purple <a href="/wiki/Lobster" title="Lobster">lobsters</a>, <a href="/wiki/Worm" title="Worm">worms</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ammonoidea" title="Ammonoidea">Ammonites</a>, spiked <a href="/wiki/Armadillo" title="Armadillo">armadillos</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bear" title="Bear">bears</a>, silver <a href="/wiki/Dragon" title="Dragon">dragons</a>, one-horned <a href="/wiki/Walrus" title="Walrus">walruses</a>, <a href="/wiki/Seahorse" title="Seahorse">seahorses</a> with feet, one-eyed <a href="/wiki/Pterodactylus" title="Pterodactylus">pterodactyls</a>, boxing glove-wearing <a href="/wiki/Gray_wolf" title="Gray wolf">wolves</a>, spiked <a href="/wiki/Spider" title="Spider">spider</a>-like <a href="/wiki/Crab" title="Crab">crabs</a>, red <a href="/wiki/Dragon" title="Dragon">dragons</a>, and brown <a href="/wiki/Wyvern" title="Wyvern">wyverns</a>.</li>
<li><b>Spirit Monsters</b> - Spirit Monsters were the last type of Monsters to be introduced in the anime. They appear as white gust-like ghostly spirits with malicious faces.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><b>Octacon</b> - A fire-breathing <a href="/wiki/Octopus" title="Octopus">octopus</a> that appeared in "Kirby Comes to Cappy Town." Octacon was the first Monster that Kirby fought. Octacon first appeared as a small octopus and ended up growing upon consuming the <a href="/wiki/Sheep" title="Sheep">sheep</a> of Cappytown. Octacon even hypnotized King Dedede. In the fight against Octacon, Kirby became Fire Kirby and destroyed Octacon.</li>
<li><b>Dedede Stone</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">デデデストーン</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Dedede Sutōn</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> - A massive statue of King Dedede that appeared in "Curio's Curious Discovery." It was unleashed by King Dedede when the Cappies wanted to toss King Dedede out of Cappy Town. It was destroyed by Stone Kirby.</li>
<li><b>Slice n' Splice</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">キッタリハッタリ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Kittarihattari</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> - Slice n' Splice is a sentient <a href="/wiki/Robot" title="Robot">robot</a> that wields a sun staff and a moon staff that can split any living thing into its male and female half. Slice n' Splice played a part in slicing Fofa into Fololo and Falala when Nightmare Enterprises sold them to King Dedede. He appeared in "The Fofa Factor" where he is ordered by King Dedede to dispose of Kirby. During this time, he remembers Fololo and Falala. Slice n' Splice is destroyed by Cutter Kirby.</li>
<li><b>Urameshiya</b> - Urameshiya is a <a href="/wiki/Ghost" title="Ghost">ghost</a> monster. It appeared in "Escargoon Squad" where it haunted Castle Dedede. It's true motive was to collect the money for the bills that King Dedede owes to Nightmare Enterprises.</li>
<li><b>Honker Stomper</b> - Honker Stomper is a monster with a large nose. King Dedede ordered him from Nightmare Enterprises in order to help find Sir Ebrum's wedding ring. His sneezes are strong enough to blow anything away. When Honker Stomper ended up in an inhaling duel, Tiff discovered that Honker Stomper was vulnerable to pepper and used it to cause Honker Stomper to lose control. King Dedede was angered upon him and Escargoon being sneezed against the wall and uses his hammer to send Honker Stomper flying.</li>
<li><b>Susshi</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">スッシー</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Susshī</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> - Susshi is a <a href="/wiki/Fish" title="Fish">fish</a>-like monster with an <a href="/wiki/Eel" title="Eel">eel</a>-like tail. In "A Princess in Dis-Dress," King Dedede uses Susshi to fight Commander Vee (who was actually Princess Rona in disguise). Kirby became Sword Kirby and helped Commander Vee into slicing off Susshi's tail.</li>
<li><b>Tornadon</b> - Tornadon is a <a href="/wiki/Slug" title="Slug">slug</a>-like monster with fan blades at the end of its arms which it uses to create tornadoes. It created a tornado that stranded Kirby, Tiff, Tuff, Fololo, and Falala on an island that was the home of Kit Cosmos. King Dedede and Escargoon arrived on Kit Cosmos' island and unleashed Tornadon on Sgt. Kit Cosmos. Kirby became Tornado Kirby and was able to destroy Tornadon.</li>
<li><b>Yamigake</b> - Yamikage is a <a href="/wiki/Ninja" title="Ninja">ninja</a> in the Galaxy Soldier Army's Ninja Special Forces until he betrayed them to Nightmare Enterprises as experienced by Meta-Knight. In "Ninja Binge", King Dedede ordered him from Nightmare Enterprises to steal back Benikage's "failing" report card (which everyone thought was a ninja scroll). Yamikage nearly killed Benikage until Kirby arrives and becomes Ninja Kirby who managed to repel Yamikage. Yamikage retreates vowing to come back and get revenge on Kirby and Meta-Knight.</li>
<li><b>WolfWrath</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">チリドッグ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Chiridoggu</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> - WolfWrath is a fuchsia <a href="/wiki/Gray_wolf" title="Gray wolf">wolf</a> which is said to have been born in the fires of <a href="/wiki/Hell" title="Hell">Hell</a> (with that fact being removed in the English dub). WolfWrath was one of Nightmare Enterprises' most powerful creations yet he doesn't take orders very well and has a weakness to water. WolfWrath once fought Meta-Knight in the past and was defeated when it fell into the lake. In "Hour of the WolfWrath", King Dedede orders WolfWrath in his latest plot to destroy Kirby. When Meta-Knight came to Kirby's aid, Meta-Knight fought WolfWrath until one of WolfWrath's attacks paralyzed Meta-Knight causing Sword Knight and Blade Knight to fight WolfWrath. Sword Knight and Blade Knight were able to drive WolfWrath into a nearby lake and Galaxia Kirby ended up destroying WolfWrath.</li>
</ul>

<tr>
<th class="navbox-group" scope="row">Spin-offs</th>
<td class="navbox-list navbox-odd hlist" style="text-align:left;border-left-width:2px;border-left-style:solid;width:100%;padding:0px">
<div style="padding:0em 0.25em">

<li><i><a href="/wiki/Kirby%27s_Block_Ball" title="Kirby's Block Ball">Block Ball</a></i></li>
